
-----title
西安
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fae66f295ab3468895900984e4d6e0e9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fae66f295ab3468895900984e4d6e0e9");'><span id='fae66f295ab3468895900984e4d6e0e9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=793&endYear=796')">793-796年</a>，20-23岁</div><div id='fae66f295ab3468895900984e4d6e0e9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=793&endYear=793')">793年7月</a>　至长安就府试。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=793&endYear=793')">793年9月</a>　执文章谒右补阙梁肃。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=795')">794-795年</a>　是年约在长安，姑系于此。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=796&endYear=796')">796年</a>　以所著文章献右司郎中杨於陵，累获称誉，有书信称谢。作品：《谢杨郎中书》<div id='poem_1372039' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372039' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372039?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢杨郎中书</a><span class='authorDate'>（796年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372039")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372039'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372039'>月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372039_comment'></div>乡贡进士李翱再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372039_comment'></div>前者以所著文章献于阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372039_comment'></div>累获咨嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372039_comment'></div>勤勤不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372039_comment'></div>翱率性多感激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372039_comment'></div>每读古贤书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372039_comment'></div>有称誉荐进后学之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372039_comment'></div>则未尝不遥想其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372039_comment'></div>若与神交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372039_comment'></div>太息悲歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372039_comment'></div>夜而复明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372039_comment'></div>何独乐已往之事哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372039_comment'></div>诚窃自悲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372039_comment'></div>临空文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372039_comment'></div>尚慨慕如不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372039_comment'></div>况亲遇厥事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372039_comment'></div>观厥人哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372039_comment'></div>幸甚幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372039_comment'></div>翱自属文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372039_comment'></div>求举有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372039_comment'></div>不获者三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372039_comment'></div>栖遑往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372039_comment'></div>困苦饥寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372039_comment'></div>踣而未能奋飞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372039_comment'></div>诚有说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372039_comment'></div>窃惟当兹之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372039_comment'></div>立行<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1372039", 1372039, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>光明</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372039_comment'></div>可以为后生之所<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1372039", 1372039, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>依归</span>者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372039_comment'></div>不过十人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372039_comment'></div>其五六人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372039_comment'></div>则本无劝诱人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372039_comment'></div>虽有卓荦奇怪之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372039_comment'></div>固不可得而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372039_comment'></div>其馀则虽或知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372039_comment'></div>欲为之荐言于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372039_comment'></div>又恐人之不我信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372039_comment'></div>因人之所不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372039_comment'></div>复生疑而不自信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372039_comment'></div>自信且犹不固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372039_comment'></div>矧曰能知人之固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372039_comment'></div>是以再往见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372039_comment'></div>或不如其初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372039_comment'></div>三往见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372039_comment'></div>又不如其再。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372039_comment'></div>若张燕公之于房太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372039_comment'></div>独孤常州之于梁补阙者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372039_comment'></div>讫不见一人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372039_comment'></div>夫如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372039_comment'></div>则非独后进者学浅词陋之罪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372039_comment'></div>抑亦先达称誉荐进之道有所不至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372039_comment'></div>孔子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372039_comment'></div>举尔所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372039_comment'></div>古君子于人之善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372039_comment'></div>惧不能知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372039_comment'></div>既知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372039_comment'></div>耻不能举之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372039_comment'></div>能举之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372039_comment'></div>耻不能成之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372039_comment'></div>若翱者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372039_comment'></div>穷贱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1372039", 1372039, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>朴讷</span>无所取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372039_comment'></div>然既为阁下之所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372039_comment'></div>敢不以古君子之道有望于阁下哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372039_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372039_comment'></div>翱载拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1372039_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='1fefa2328be74aa697a0a707a0288840_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1fefa2328be74aa697a0a707a0288840");'><span id='1fefa2328be74aa697a0a707a0288840_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=797&endYear=797')">797年</a>，24岁</div><div id='1fefa2328be74aa697a0a707a0288840' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=797&endYear=797')">797年</a>　四举进士下第，有赋作追思梁肃之相知并自伤。作品：《感知己赋并序》<div id='poem_1372015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372015?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感知巳赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（797年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372015")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372015_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1372015'>贞元九年。翱始就州府之贡举人事。其九月。执文章一通。谒于右补阙安定梁君。是时梁君之誉塞天下。属词求进之士。奉文章造梁君门下者。盖无虚日。梁君知人之过也。亦既相见。遂于翱有相知之道焉。谓翱得古人之遗风。期翱之名不朽于无穷。许翱以拂拭吹嘘。翱初谓面相进也。亦未幸甚。十一月。梁君遘疾而殁。翱渐游于朋友公卿间。往往皆曰。吾久籍子姓名于补阙梁君也。翱乃知非面相进也。当时意谓先进者遇人特达。皆合有是心。亦未谓知巳之难得也。梁君殁于兹五年。翱学圣人经籍教训文句之旨。而为文将数万言。愈昔年见于梁君之文。弗啻数倍。虽不敢同德于古人。然亦常无怍于中心。每岁试于礼部。连以文章罢黜。声光晦昧于时俗。人皆谓之固宜。然后知先进者遇人特达。亦不皆有是心也。方知知巳之难得也。夫见善而不能知。虽善何为。知而不能誉。则如勿知。誉而不能深。则如勿誉。深而不能久。则如弗深。久而不能终。则如勿久。翱虽不肖。幸辱于梁君所知。君为之言于人。岂非誉欤。谓其有古人之风。岂非深欤。誉而逮夫终身。岂非久欤。不幸梁君短命遽殁。是以翱未能有成也。其谁能相继梁君之志而成之欤。巳焉哉。天之遽丧梁君也。是使翱之命久迍邅厄穷也。遂赋感知巳以自伤。其言怨而不乱。盖小雅骚人之馀风也。其辞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1372015_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372015'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372015'>戚戚之愁苦兮。思释去之无端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372015_comment'></div>彼众人之容易兮。乃志士之所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372015_comment'></div>伊自古皆嗟兮。又何怨乎兹之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372015_comment'></div>独厄穷而不达兮。悼知音之永逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372015_comment'></div>纷予生之多故兮。愧特于世之谁知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372015_comment'></div>抚圣人教化之旨兮。洵合古而乖时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372015_comment'></div>诚自负其中心兮。嗟与俗而相违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372015_comment'></div>趋一名之五稔兮。尚无成而淹此路岐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372015_comment'></div>昔圣贤之遑遑兮。极屈辱之驱驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372015_comment'></div>择中庸之难蹈兮。虽困顿而终不改其所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372015_comment'></div>苟天地之无私兮。曷不鉴照于神祇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372015_comment'></div>心劲直于松柏兮。沦霜雪而不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372015_comment'></div>知我者忽然逝兮。岂吾道之巳而。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372015_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1372015_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2ebcd5d33b0a455dbe99796d90e4e252_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2ebcd5d33b0a455dbe99796d90e4e252");'><span id='2ebcd5d33b0a455dbe99796d90e4e252_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=797&endYear=798')">797-798年</a>，24-25岁</div><div id='2ebcd5d33b0a455dbe99796d90e4e252' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=797&endYear=797')">797年</a>　秋，又至长安赴进士试。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>　春，进士擢第，知贡举顾少连。作品：《鉴止水赋》《青出蓝诗》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=798&endYear=798')">798年</a>　有文赠落第西行成都的冯定。作品：《送冯定序》<div id='poem_1372049' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372049' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372049?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送冯定序</a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372049")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372049'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372049'>冯生自负其气而中立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372049_comment'></div>上无援。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372049_comment'></div>下无交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372049_comment'></div>名声未大耀于京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372049_comment'></div>生信无罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372049_comment'></div>是乃时之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372049_comment'></div>见之者或不能知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372049_comment'></div>知之者则不敢言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372049_comment'></div>是以再举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372049_comment'></div>皆不如其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372049_comment'></div>谓生无戚戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372049_comment'></div>盖以他人为解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372049_comment'></div>予联以杂文罢黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372049_comment'></div>不知者亦纷纷交笑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372049_comment'></div>其自负益明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372049_comment'></div>退学书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372049_comment'></div>感愤而为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372049_comment'></div>遂遭知音成其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372049_comment'></div>当黜辱时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372049_comment'></div>吾不言其拙也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372049_comment'></div>岂无命耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372049_comment'></div>及既得时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372049_comment'></div>吾又不自言其智也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372049_comment'></div>岂有命耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372049_comment'></div>故谓生无戚戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372049_comment'></div>生家贫甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372049_comment'></div>不能居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372049_comment'></div>告我游成都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372049_comment'></div>成都有岷峨山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372049_comment'></div>合气于江源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372049_comment'></div>往往出奇怪之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372049_comment'></div>古有司马相如扬雄严君平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372049_comment'></div>其人死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372049_comment'></div>至兹千年不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372049_comment'></div>生游成都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372049_comment'></div>试为我谢岷峨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372049_comment'></div>何其久无人耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372049_comment'></div>其风<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1372049", 1372049, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>侈丽</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1372049", 1372049, "Clauses/37/Comments/1")'>奢豪</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372049_comment'></div>羁人易留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372049_comment'></div>生其思速出于剑门之艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372049_comment'></div>勿我忧也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1372049_comment'></div></div></div><br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=811&endYear=811')">811年</a>　因事至京师，晤张籍。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='e1b716c1226849afb3414384679b6947_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e1b716c1226849afb3414384679b6947");'><span id='e1b716c1226849afb3414384679b6947_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=820')">817-820年</a>，44-47岁</div><div id='e1b716c1226849afb3414384679b6947' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　行至京师，冬，逢卢坦归葬路过京师，李翱有祭文并随后作传。作品：《祭故东川卢大夫文、故东川节度使卢公传》<div id='poem_1372109' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372109' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372109?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭故东川卢大夫文</a><span class='authorDate'>（817年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372109")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372109_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372109'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372109'>前此八年。公在宣州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372109_comment'></div>翱归自南。下江之流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372109_comment'></div>公发辟书。使者来召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372109_comment'></div>言重礼至。实宾之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372109_comment'></div>内惧不称。又安敢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372109_comment'></div>仰公之德。自托如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372109_comment'></div>亦既在门。有言必信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372109_comment'></div>翱亦不贰。知贤则进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372109_comment'></div>公曰汝言。我用无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372109_comment'></div>每疑贤者。患不能知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372109_comment'></div>汝正而公。与我气合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372109_comment'></div>有怀必陈。无谓弗纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372109_comment'></div>公迁侍郎。翱赴浙东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372109_comment'></div>宦途有阻。困不能通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372109_comment'></div>公陈上前。出白丞相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372109_comment'></div>保明无过。炤灼有状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372109_comment'></div>事遂解释。奏方成官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372109_comment'></div>非公之力。其退于田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372109_comment'></div>公镇剑州。翱亦东掾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372109_comment'></div>亟言于相。曷不以荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372109_comment'></div>官罢在家。卧病<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1372109", 1372109, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>饮贫</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372109_comment'></div>惟公见念。复召为宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372109_comment'></div>自修<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1372109", 1372109, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>辟牒</span>。以复前好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372109_comment'></div>承命而行。不惮远道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372109_comment'></div>余及陕郊。闻公之丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372109_comment'></div>失声泣哭。若火煎肠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372109_comment'></div>公为大臣。一心正直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372109_comment'></div>发言动听。义形在色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372109_comment'></div>公出乎外。众论日归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372109_comment'></div>辅相之位。实公所宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372109_comment'></div>惟公之薨。骨鲠道衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372109_comment'></div>天下失望。贤人共悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372109_comment'></div>生必有尽。自古皆尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372109_comment'></div>殁而益光。孰与公比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372109_comment'></div>丧车东去。归祔先址。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372109_comment'></div>临路一号。永诀于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372109_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372109_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1372109_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　在长安，冬，为国子博士、史馆修撰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=818&endYear=818')">818年</a>　在长安，有书上宰相裴度，反对其亲征淄青节度使李师道。作品：《劝裴相不自出征书》<div id='poem_1372037' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372037' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372037?labeling=true' target='_blank'>劝裴相不自出征书</a><span class='authorDate'>（818年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372037")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372037_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372037'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372037'>三两日来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372037_comment'></div>皆传阁下以淄青未平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372037_comment'></div>又请东讨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372037_comment'></div>虽非指的。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372037_comment'></div>或虑未实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372037_comment'></div>万一者有之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372037_comment'></div>只可先事而言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372037_comment'></div>岂得后而有悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372037_comment'></div>且如房杜姚宋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372037_comment'></div>时政大耀而无武功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372037_comment'></div>郭汾阳二李太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372037_comment'></div>立大勋而不当国政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372037_comment'></div>阁下以舍人使魏博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372037_comment'></div>六州之地归矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372037_comment'></div>自秉大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372037_comment'></div>兵诛蔡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372037_comment'></div>久而不克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372037_comment'></div>奉命宣慰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372037_comment'></div>未经时而吴元济生擒矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372037_comment'></div>使一布衣持书涉河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372037_comment'></div>而王承宗恐惧委命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372037_comment'></div>割地以献矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372037_comment'></div>自武德以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372037_comment'></div>宰相居庙堂而成就功业者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372037_comment'></div>未有其比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372037_comment'></div>是宜以功成身退养德善守为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372037_comment'></div>奈何如始进之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372037_comment'></div>汲汲于功名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372037_comment'></div>复欲出征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372037_comment'></div>以速平寇贼之为事耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372037_comment'></div>自秦汉以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372037_comment'></div>亦未尝有立大功而不知止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372037_comment'></div>能保其终者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372037_comment'></div>即韩侍中亲率重兵以压境矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372037_comment'></div>田司空深入贼地以立功矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372037_comment'></div>凡人之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372037_comment'></div>亦各欲成功在己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372037_comment'></div>惟恐居下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372037_comment'></div>顾宰相衔命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372037_comment'></div>领三数书生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372037_comment'></div>指麾来临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372037_comment'></div>坐而享其功名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372037_comment'></div>夺人之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372037_comment'></div>不可一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372037_comment'></div>功高不赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372037_comment'></div>不可二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372037_comment'></div>兵者危道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372037_comment'></div>万一旬月不即如志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372037_comment'></div>是坐弃前劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372037_comment'></div>不可三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372037_comment'></div>凡三事昭灼易见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372037_comment'></div>岂或事在于己而云未熟耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372037_comment'></div>伏望试以狂言访于所知之厚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372037_comment'></div>意切辞尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372037_comment'></div>不暇文饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372037_comment'></div>伏惟少赐省察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372037_comment'></div>翱再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_56_1372037_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　在长安，上书宰相崔群指其未尽谏诤之责。作品：《论事于宰相书》<div id='poem_1372036' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372036' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372036?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论事于宰相书</a><span class='authorDate'>（819年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372036")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372036_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372036'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372036'>凡居上位之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372036_comment'></div>皆勇于进而懦于退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372036_comment'></div>但见已道之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372036_comment'></div>不见己道之塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372036_comment'></div>日度一日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372036_comment'></div>以至于黜退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372036_comment'></div>奄至而终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372036_comment'></div>不能先自为谋者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372036_comment'></div>前后皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372036_comment'></div>阁下居位三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372036_comment'></div>其所合于人情者不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372036_comment'></div>其所乖于物议者亦已多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372036_comment'></div>奸邪登用而不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372036_comment'></div>知而不能去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372036_comment'></div>柳泌为刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372036_comment'></div>疏而不止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372036_comment'></div>韩潮州直谏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1372036", 1372036, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>贬责</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372036_comment'></div>诤而不得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372036_comment'></div>道路之人咸曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372036_comment'></div>焉用彼相矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372036_comment'></div>阁下尚自恕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372036_comment'></div>以为犹可以辅政太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372036_comment'></div>虽枉尺犹能直寻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372036_comment'></div>较吾所得者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372036_comment'></div>不啻补其所失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372036_comment'></div>何足遽自为去就也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372036_comment'></div>窃怪阁下能容忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372036_comment'></div>亦已甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372036_comment'></div>昨日来高枕不寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372036_comment'></div>静为阁下思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372036_comment'></div>岂有宰相上三疏而止一邪人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372036_comment'></div>而终不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372036_comment'></div>阁下天资畏慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372036_comment'></div>又不能显辩其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372036_comment'></div>忍耻署敕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372036_comment'></div>内愧私叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372036_comment'></div>又将自恕曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372036_comment'></div>吾道尚行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372036_comment'></div>吾言尚信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372036_comment'></div>我果为贤相矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372036_comment'></div>我若引退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372036_comment'></div>则谁能辅太平耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372036_comment'></div>是又不可之甚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372036_comment'></div>当贞观之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372036_comment'></div>房杜为相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372036_comment'></div>以为非房杜则不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372036_comment'></div>开元之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372036_comment'></div>姚宋为相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372036_comment'></div>以为非姚宋则不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372036_comment'></div>房杜姚宋之不为相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372036_comment'></div>亦已久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372036_comment'></div>中书未尝无宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372036_comment'></div>然则果何必于房杜姚宋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372036_comment'></div>况道不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372036_comment'></div>虽皋陶伊尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372036_comment'></div>将何为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372036_comment'></div>房杜姚宋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372036_comment'></div>诚贤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372036_comment'></div>若道不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372036_comment'></div>言不信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372036_comment'></div>其心所谓贤者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372036_comment'></div>终不敢不进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372036_comment'></div>其心所谓邪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372036_comment'></div>终不敢不辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372036_comment'></div>而许敬宗李义府同列用事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372036_comment'></div>言信道行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372036_comment'></div>又自度智力必不足以排之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372036_comment'></div>则将自引而止乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372036_comment'></div>将坐而待黜退乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372036_comment'></div>尚自恕苟安于位乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372036_comment'></div>以阁下之明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372036_comment'></div>度之当可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372036_comment'></div>凡虑己事则不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1372036_comment'></div>断他人事则明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1372036_comment'></div>已私而他人公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1372036_comment'></div>勇易断也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1372036_comment'></div>承阁下厚知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1372036_comment'></div>受<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1372036", 1372036, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>奖擢</span>者不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1372036_comment'></div>能受阁下德而献<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_78_1372036", 1372036, "Clauses/78/Comments/0")'>尽言</span>者未必多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1372036_comment'></div>人幸蒙以国士见目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1372036_comment'></div>十五年馀矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1372036_comment'></div>但欲自竭其分耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1372036_comment'></div>听与怪在阁下裁之而已。</div><div id='poem_sentence_82_1372036_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　在长安，秋，上疏论六事。作品：《论事疏表》《疏用忠正》《疏屏奸佞》《疏绝进献》《疏厚边兵》《数引见待制官问以时事》<div id='poem_1372021' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372021' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372021?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论事疏表<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>疏用忠正</a><span class='authorDate'>（819年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372021")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372021_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372021'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372021'>臣闻国之所以兴者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372021_comment'></div>主能信任大臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372021_comment'></div>臣能以忠正辅主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372021_comment'></div>故忠正者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372021_comment'></div>百行之宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372021_comment'></div>大臣忠正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372021_comment'></div>则小臣莫敢不为正矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372021_comment'></div>小臣莫敢不为正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372021_comment'></div>则天下后进之士皆乐忠正之道矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372021_comment'></div>后进之士皆乐行忠正之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372021_comment'></div>是王化之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372021_comment'></div>太平之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372021_comment'></div>今之语者必曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372021_comment'></div>知人邪正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372021_comment'></div>是尧舜之所难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372021_comment'></div>焉得知忠正之人而用之耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372021_comment'></div>臣以为察忠正之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372021_comment'></div>盖有术焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372021_comment'></div>能尽言忧国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372021_comment'></div>而不希恩容者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372021_comment'></div>此忠正之徒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372021_comment'></div>夫忠正之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372021_comment'></div>亦各自有党类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372021_comment'></div>邪臣嫉而谗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372021_comment'></div>必且以为相朋党矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372021_comment'></div>夫舜禹稷契之相称赞也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372021_comment'></div>不为朋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372021_comment'></div>颜闵之相往来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372021_comment'></div>不为党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372021_comment'></div>皆在于讲道德仁义而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372021_comment'></div>邪人嫉而谗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372021_comment'></div>且以为朋党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372021_comment'></div>用以惑时主之听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372021_comment'></div>从古以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372021_comment'></div>皆有之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372021_comment'></div>故萧望之周堪刘向谋退许史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372021_comment'></div>竟为邪臣所胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372021_comment'></div>汉元帝不能辨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372021_comment'></div>而终任用邪臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372021_comment'></div>汉室之衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372021_comment'></div>始于元帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372021_comment'></div>此不可不察也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372021_comment'></div>故听其言能数逆于耳者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372021_comment'></div>忠正之臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372021_comment'></div>虽任之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372021_comment'></div>杂以邪佞之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372021_comment'></div>则太平必不能成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372021_comment'></div>文宣王曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372021_comment'></div>十室之邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372021_comment'></div>必有忠信如某者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372021_comment'></div>故忠信之人不难有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372021_comment'></div>在陛下辨而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372021_comment'></div>各以类进之而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372021_comment'></div>臣故曰用忠正而不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372021_comment'></div>则功德成。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1372021_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1372022' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372022' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372022?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>疏屏奸佞</a><span class='authorDate'>（819年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372022_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372022'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372022'>臣闻孔子远佞人。言不可以共为国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372022_comment'></div>凡自古奸佞之人可辨也。皆不知大体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372022_comment'></div>不怀远虑。务于利巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372022_comment'></div>贪富贵。固荣宠而巳矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372022_comment'></div>必好甘言谄辞。以希人主之欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372022_comment'></div>主之所贵。因而贤之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372022_comment'></div>主之所怒。因而罪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372022_comment'></div>主好利。则献蓄聚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1372022", 1372022, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>敛剥</span>之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372022_comment'></div>主好声色。则开妖艳郑卫之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372022_comment'></div>主好神仙。则通烧鍊变化之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372022_comment'></div>望主之色。希主之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372022_comment'></div>顺主之言。而奉承之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372022_comment'></div>人主悦其不违于巳。因而亲之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372022_comment'></div>以至于事失怨生而不闻也。若事失怨生而不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372022_comment'></div>其危也深矣。自古奸邪之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372022_comment'></div>未有不如此者也。然则虽尧舜为君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372022_comment'></div>稷契为臣。而杂之以奸邪之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372022_comment'></div>则太平必不可兴。而危事潜生矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372022_comment'></div>所谓奸邪之臣者。荣夷公费无极太宰噽王子兰王凤张禹许敬宗杨再思李义府李林甫卢裴延龄之比是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372022_comment'></div>奸佞之臣信用。大则亡国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372022_comment'></div>小则坏法度而乱生矣。今之语者必曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372022_comment'></div>知人邪正。是尧舜之所难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372022_comment'></div>焉得知其邪佞而去之耶。臣以为察奸佞之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372022_comment'></div>亦有术焉。主之所欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372022_comment'></div>皆顺不违。又从而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1372022", 1372022, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>承奉</span>先后之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372022_comment'></div>此奸佞之臣也。不去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372022_comment'></div>虽用稷契为相。不能以致太平矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372022_comment'></div>故人主之任奸佞。则耳目壅蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372022_comment'></div>耳目壅蔽。则过不闻而忠正不进矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372022_comment'></div>臣故曰屏奸佞而不近。则视听聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372022_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_1372022_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1372024' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372024' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372024?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>疏绝进献</a><span class='authorDate'>（819年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372024_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372024'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372024'>臣以为自建中以来。税法不更。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372024_comment'></div>百姓之困。巳备于前篇矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372024_comment'></div>今节度观察使之进献。必曰军府羡馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372024_comment'></div>不取于百姓。且供军及留州钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372024_comment'></div>各有定额。若非兵士阙数不填。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372024_comment'></div>及<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1372024", 1372024, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>减刻</span>所给。则钱帛非天之所雨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372024_comment'></div>非如泉之可涌而生也。不取于百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372024_comment'></div>将安取之哉。故有作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1372024", 1372024, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>官店</span>以居商贾者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372024_comment'></div>有酿酒而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1372024", 1372024, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>官沽</span>者。其他杂率。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372024_comment'></div>巧设名号。是皆夺百姓之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372024_comment'></div>亏三代之法。公托进献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372024_comment'></div>因得自成其私。甚非太平之事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372024_comment'></div>比年天下皆厚留度支钱蓄兵士者。以中原之有寇贼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372024_comment'></div>今吴元济李师道皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1372024", 1372024, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>枭斩</span>矣。中原无虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372024_comment'></div>而蓄兵如故。以耗百姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372024_comment'></div>臣以为非是也。若选通达吏事之臣三五人往诸道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372024_comment'></div>与其节度使团练使言。每道要留兵数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372024_comment'></div>以备镇守。责其兵士见在实数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372024_comment'></div>因使其逃亡不补。自可以每年十销一矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372024_comment'></div>告之以中原无事。蕃夷可虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372024_comment'></div>每道宜配兵若干。取其衣粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372024_comment'></div>以赐边兵。而召战士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372024_comment'></div>使边兵实。则蕃夷不足虑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372024_comment'></div>夫钱帛皆国家之钱帛也。宜作明法以取之是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372024_comment'></div>若使通达吏事之臣往使焉。虽其将帅之不尽诚者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372024_comment'></div>亦不敢有所隐矣。今受进献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372024_comment'></div>则节度使团练使皆多方刻下为蓄聚。其自为私者三分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372024_comment'></div>其所进献者一分也。是岂非两税之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372024_comment'></div>又加税焉。百姓之所不乐其业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372024_comment'></div>而父子夫妇或有不能相养矣。父子夫妇不能相养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372024_comment'></div>而望太平之兴。虽妇人女子皆知其未可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372024_comment'></div>臣故曰绝进献以宽百姓税租之重。则下不困。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372024_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1372024_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1372025' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372025' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372025?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>疏厚边兵</a><span class='authorDate'>（819年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372025_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372025'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372025'>臣以为方今中原无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372025_comment'></div>其虑者蕃戎与北虏而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372025_comment'></div>议者以为边备尚虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372025_comment'></div>皆可忧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372025_comment'></div>兵法有之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372025_comment'></div>不恃敌之不来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372025_comment'></div>恃此之不可胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372025_comment'></div>今国家威武达于四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372025_comment'></div>其不敢犯边为寇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372025_comment'></div>虽巳明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372025_comment'></div>然蕃戎如犬羊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372025_comment'></div>安识礼义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372025_comment'></div>而必其不为寇哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372025_comment'></div>且去岁犯边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372025_comment'></div>足以明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372025_comment'></div>臣以为使缘边诸节度使特共召战士十万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372025_comment'></div>每岁不过费钱一百万贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372025_comment'></div>则边备实矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372025_comment'></div>边上有召战之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372025_comment'></div>达于四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372025_comment'></div>四夷心服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372025_comment'></div>不敢为盗矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372025_comment'></div>四夷不敢为盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372025_comment'></div>边鄙之人得无兵战之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372025_comment'></div>则京师可高枕而视矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1372025_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　在长安，曾上书论太庙朔望上食。作品：《陵庙日时朔祭议》<div id='poem_1378557' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1378557' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1378557?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陵庙日时朔祭议</a><span class='authorDate'>（819年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1378557")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1378557_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1378557'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1378557'>徵事郎守国子博士史馆修撰臣李翱等谨献议曰。国语曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1378557_comment'></div>王者日祭。礼记曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1378557_comment'></div>王立七庙。皆月祭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1378557_comment'></div>周礼不载日祭月祭。惟四时之祭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1378557_comment'></div>礿祠蒸尝。汉朝皆杂而用之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1378557_comment'></div>盖遭秦火。诗书礼经烬灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1378557_comment'></div>编残缺。汉乃求之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1378557_comment'></div>先儒穿凿。各伸巳见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1378557_comment'></div>皆托古圣贤之名。以信其语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1378557_comment'></div>故其所记。各不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1378557_comment'></div>古者庙有寝而不墓祭。秦汉始建寝庙于园陵而上食焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1378557_comment'></div>国家因之而不改。贞观开元礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1378557_comment'></div>并无宗庙日祭月祭之礼。盖以日祭月祭既巳行于陵寝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1378557_comment'></div>故太庙之中。每岁五享六告而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1378557_comment'></div>不然者。房玄龄魏徵之辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1378557_comment'></div>皆一代名臣。穷极经史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1378557_comment'></div>岂不见国语礼记有日祭月祭之辞乎。斯足以明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1378557_comment'></div>伏以太庙之享。笾豆牲牢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1378557_comment'></div>三代之通礼。是贵诚之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1378557_comment'></div>园寝之奠。改用常馔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1378557_comment'></div>秦汉之权制。乃食味之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1378557_comment'></div>今朔望上食于陵寝。修秦汉故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1378557_comment'></div>斯为可矣。若朔望上食于太庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1378557_comment'></div>岂非用常亵味而贵多品乎。且非礼所谓至敬不享味而贵气臭之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1378557_comment'></div>传称屈到嗜芰。有疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1378557_comment'></div>召其宗老而属之曰。祭我必以芰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1378557_comment'></div>及祭荐芰。屈建命去芰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1378557_comment'></div>而用羊馈笾豆脯醢。君子是之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1378557_comment'></div>言事祖考之义。当以礼为重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1378557_comment'></div>不以其生存所嗜为献。盖明非食味也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1378557_comment'></div>然则荐常馔于太庙。无乃与荐芰为比乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1378557_comment'></div>且非三代圣王之所行也。况祭器不设俎豆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1378557_comment'></div>祭官不命三公。执事者惟宫闱令宗正卿而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1378557_comment'></div>谓之上食可也。安得以为祭乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1378557_comment'></div>且时享于太庙。有司摄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1378557_comment'></div>祝文曰。孝曾孙皇帝臣某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1378557_comment'></div>谨遣太尉臣名。敢昭告于高祖神尧皇帝祖妣太穆皇后窦氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1378557_comment'></div>时维孟春。永怀罔极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1378557_comment'></div>谨以一元大武柔毛<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1378557", 1378557, "Clauses/76/Comments/0")'>刚鬣</span>明粢芗萁<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1378557", 1378557, "Clauses/76/Comments/1")'>嘉蔬</span>醴齐。敬修嘉荐时享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1378557_comment'></div>以申追慕。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1378557", 1378557, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>尚飨</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1378557_comment'></div>此祝词也。前享七日质明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1378557_comment'></div>太尉誓百官于尚书省曰。某日时享于太庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1378557_comment'></div>各扬其职。不供其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1378557_comment'></div>国有常刑。凡陪享之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1378557_comment'></div>散斋四日。致斋三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1378557_comment'></div>然后乃可以为祭也。宗庙之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1378557_comment'></div>非敢擅议。虽有知者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1378557_comment'></div>其谁敢言。故六十馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1378557_comment'></div>行之不废。今圣朝以弓矢既櫜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1378557_comment'></div>礼乐为大。故下百僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1378557_comment'></div>使得详议。臣等以为贞观开元礼并无太庙上食之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1378557_comment'></div>以礼节情。罢之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1378557_comment'></div>至若陵寝上食。采国语礼记日祭月祭之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1378557_comment'></div>因秦汉之制。修而存之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1378557_comment'></div>以广孝道可也。如此则经义可据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1378557_comment'></div>故事不遗。大礼既明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1378557_comment'></div>永息异论。可以继二帝三王而为万代法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1378557_comment'></div>与其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1378557", 1378557, "Clauses/114/Comments/0")'>黩礼</span>越古。贵因循而惮改作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1378557_comment'></div>犹天地之相远也。谨议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1378557_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_59_1378557_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=819&endYear=819')">819年</a>　在长安，奏请作行状不得虚说礼智仁义，宪宗从其言，李翱遂转考功员外郎。作品：《百官行状奏》<div id='poem_1372019' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372019' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372019?labeling=true' target='_blank'>百官行状奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（819年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372019")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372019_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372019'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372019'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372019_comment'></div>臣等无能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372019_comment'></div>谬得秉笔史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372019_comment'></div>以记注为职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372019_comment'></div>夫劝善惩恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372019_comment'></div>正言直笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372019_comment'></div>纪圣朝功德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372019_comment'></div>述忠臣贤士事业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372019_comment'></div>载奸臣佞人丑行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372019_comment'></div>以传无穷者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372019_comment'></div>史官之任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372019_comment'></div>伏以陛下即位十五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372019_comment'></div>乃元年平夏州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372019_comment'></div>二年平蜀斩辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372019_comment'></div>三年平江东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372019_comment'></div>斩锜张茂昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372019_comment'></div>遂得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1372019", 1372019, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>易定</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372019_comment'></div>五年擒史宪诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372019_comment'></div>得泽潞邢洺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372019_comment'></div>七年田宏正以魏博六州来受常贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372019_comment'></div>十二年平淮西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372019_comment'></div>斩元济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372019_comment'></div>十三年王承宗献德棣入税租。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372019_comment'></div>沧景除吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372019_comment'></div>十四年平淄青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372019_comment'></div>斩师道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372019_comment'></div>得十二州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372019_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1372019", 1372019, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>神断</span>武功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372019_comment'></div>自古中兴之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372019_comment'></div>莫有及者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372019_comment'></div>而自元和以来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372019_comment'></div>未著实录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372019_comment'></div>盛德大功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372019_comment'></div>史氏未纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372019_comment'></div>忠臣贤士名德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372019_comment'></div>甚有可为法者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372019_comment'></div>逆臣贼人丑行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372019_comment'></div>亦有可为诫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372019_comment'></div>史氏皆阙而未书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372019_comment'></div>臣实惧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372019_comment'></div>故不自量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372019_comment'></div>辄欲勉强而修之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372019_comment'></div>凡人之事迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372019_comment'></div>非大善大恶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372019_comment'></div>则众人无由知之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372019_comment'></div>故旧例皆访问于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372019_comment'></div>又取<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1372019", 1372019, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>行状</span>谥议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372019_comment'></div>以为一据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372019_comment'></div>今之作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1372019", 1372019, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>行状</span>者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372019_comment'></div>非其门生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372019_comment'></div>即其故吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372019_comment'></div>莫不虚加仁义礼智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372019_comment'></div>妄言忠肃惠和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372019_comment'></div>或言盛德大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372019_comment'></div>远而愈光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372019_comment'></div>或云直道正言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372019_comment'></div>殁而不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372019_comment'></div>曾不直叙其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372019_comment'></div>故善恶混然不可明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372019_comment'></div>至如许敬宗李义府李林甫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372019_comment'></div>国朝之奸臣也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372019_comment'></div>其使门生故吏作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1372019", 1372019, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>行状</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372019_comment'></div>既不指其事实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372019_comment'></div>虚称道忠信以加之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372019_comment'></div>则可以移之于房玄龄魏徵裴炎徐有功矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372019_comment'></div>此不惟其处心不实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372019_comment'></div>苟欲虚美于所受恩之地而巳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372019_comment'></div>盖亦为文者又非游夏迁雄之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372019_comment'></div>务于华而忘其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372019_comment'></div>溺于辞而弃其理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372019_comment'></div>故为文则失六经之古风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372019_comment'></div>记事则非史迁之实录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372019_comment'></div>不如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1372019_comment'></div>则辞句鄙陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1372019_comment'></div>不能自成其文矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1372019_comment'></div>由是事失其本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1372019_comment'></div>文害于理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1372019_comment'></div>而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1372019", 1372019, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>行状</span>不足以取信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1372019_comment'></div>若使指事书实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1372019_comment'></div>不饰虚言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1372019_comment'></div>则必有人知其真伪不然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1372019_comment'></div>纵使门生故吏为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1372019_comment'></div>亦不可以谬作德善之事而加之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1372019_comment'></div>臣今请作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_83_1372019", 1372019, "Clauses/83/Comments/0")'>行状</span>者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1372019_comment'></div>不要虚说仁义礼智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1372019_comment'></div>忠肃惠和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1372019_comment'></div>盛德大业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1372019_comment'></div>正言直道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1372019_comment'></div>芜秽册。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1372019_comment'></div>不可取信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1372019_comment'></div>但指事说实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1372019_comment'></div>直载其词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1372019_comment'></div>则善恶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1372019", 1372019, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>功迹</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1372019_comment'></div>皆据事足以自见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1372019_comment'></div>假令传魏徵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1372019_comment'></div>但记其谏争之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1372019_comment'></div>足以为正直矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1372019_comment'></div>如传段秀实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1372019_comment'></div>但记其倒用司农寺印以追逆兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1372019_comment'></div>又以象笏击朱泚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1372019_comment'></div>自足以为忠烈矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1372019_comment'></div>今之为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_101_1372019", 1372019, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>行状</span>者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1372019_comment'></div>都不指其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1372019_comment'></div>率以虚词称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1372019_comment'></div>故无魏徵之谏争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1372019_comment'></div>而加之以正直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1372019_comment'></div>无秀实之义勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1372019_comment'></div>而加之以忠烈者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1372019_comment'></div>皆是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1372019_comment'></div>其何足以为据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1372019_comment'></div>若考功视<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_110_1372019", 1372019, "Clauses/110/Comments/0")'>行状</span>之不依此者不得受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1372019_comment'></div>依此者乃下太常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1372019_comment'></div>并牒史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1372019_comment'></div>太常定谥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1372019_comment'></div>牒送史馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1372019_comment'></div>则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_115_1372019", 1372019, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>行状</span>之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1372019_comment'></div>纵未可一一皆信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1372019_comment'></div>与其虚加妄言都无事实者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1372019_comment'></div>犹山泽高下之不同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1372019_comment'></div>史氏记录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1372019_comment'></div>须得本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1372019_comment'></div>苟凭往例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1372019_comment'></div>皆是空言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1372019_comment'></div>则使史馆何所为据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1372019_comment'></div>伏乞下臣此奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1372019_comment'></div>使考功守行善恶之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1372019_comment'></div>虽故吏门生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1372019_comment'></div>亦不能虚作而加之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1372019_comment'></div>臣等要知事实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1372019_comment'></div>辄敢陈论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1372019_comment'></div>轻黩天威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1372019_comment'></div>无任战越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1372019_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_132_1372019_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=820&endYear=820')">820年</a>　与因凌蔑公卿贬为建州刺史的李景俭相善，坐贬朗州刺史。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='9b68c4cb67b74ec7a3607783217f87c4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9b68c4cb67b74ec7a3607783217f87c4");'><span id='9b68c4cb67b74ec7a3607783217f87c4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=825')">824-825年</a>，51-52岁</div><div id='9b68c4cb67b74ec7a3607783217f87c4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>　在礼部郎中任，夏，韩愈请告养疾城南庄，李翱时与韩愈相晤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年12月2日</a>　在礼部郎中任，韩愈卒，李翱作行状，叙其官历事迹请中书牒考功下太常定谥。作品：《故正议大夫行尚书吏部侍郎上柱国赐紫金鱼袋赠礼部尚书韩公行状》<div id='poem_1372103' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372103' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372103?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故正议大夫行尚书吏部侍郎上柱国赐紫金鱼袋赠礼部尚书韩公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（824年12月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372103")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372103_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372103'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372103'>曾祖泰。皇任曹州司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372103_comment'></div>祖浚素。皇任桂州长史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372103_comment'></div>父仲卿。皇任秘书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372103_comment'></div>赠尚书左仆射。公讳愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372103_comment'></div>字退之。昌黎人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372103_comment'></div>生三岁父殁。养于兄会舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372103_comment'></div>及长读书。能记他生之所习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372103_comment'></div>年二十五上进士第。汴州乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372103_comment'></div>诏以旧相东都留守董晋为平章事宣武军节度使。以平汴州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372103_comment'></div>晋辟公以行。遂入汴州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372103_comment'></div>得试秘书省校书郎。为观察推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372103_comment'></div>晋卒。公从晋丧以出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372103_comment'></div>四日而汴州乱。凡从事之居者皆杀死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372103_comment'></div>武宁军节度使张建封奏为节度推官。得试太常寺协律郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372103_comment'></div>选授四门博士。迁监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372103_comment'></div>为幸臣所恶。出守连州阳山令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372103_comment'></div>政有惠于下。及公去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372103_comment'></div>百姓多以公之姓以命其子。改江陵府法曹参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372103_comment'></div>入为权知国子博士。宰相有爱公文者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372103_comment'></div>将以文学职处公。有争先者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372103_comment'></div>搆公语以非之。公恐及难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372103_comment'></div>遂求分司东都。权知三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372103_comment'></div>改真博士。入省为分司都官员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372103_comment'></div>改河南县令。日以职分辨于留守及尹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372103_comment'></div>故军士莫敢犯禁。入为职方员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372103_comment'></div>华州刺史奏华阴县令柳涧有罪。遂将贬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372103_comment'></div>公上疏请发御史辩曲直。方可处以罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372103_comment'></div>则下不受屈。既柳涧有犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372103_comment'></div>公由是复为国子博士。改比部郎中史馆修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372103_comment'></div>转考功郎中。修撰如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372103_comment'></div>数月以考功知制诰。上将平蔡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372103_comment'></div>先命御史中丞裴公度使诸军以视兵。及还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372103_comment'></div>奏兵可用。贼势可以灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372103_comment'></div>颇与宰相意忤。既数月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372103_comment'></div>盗杀宰相。又害中丞不克。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372103_comment'></div>中丞微伤。马逸以免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372103_comment'></div>遂为宰相。以主东兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372103_comment'></div>自安禄山起范阳。陷两京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372103_comment'></div>河南北七镇节度使。身死则立其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372103_comment'></div>作军士表以请。朝廷因而与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372103_comment'></div>及贞元季年。虽顺地节将死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372103_comment'></div>多即军中取行军副使将校以授之节。习以成故矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372103_comment'></div>朝廷之贤。恬然于所安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372103_comment'></div>以苟不用兵为贵。议多与裴丞相异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372103_comment'></div>唯公以为盗杀宰相。而遂息兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372103_comment'></div>其为懦甚大。兵不可以息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372103_comment'></div>以天下力取三州。尚何不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372103_comment'></div>与裴丞相议合。故兵遂用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372103_comment'></div>而宰相有不便之者。月满迁中书舍人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372103_comment'></div>赐绯鱼袋。后竟以他事改太子右庶子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372103_comment'></div>元和十三年秋。以兵老久屯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372103_comment'></div>贼未灭。上命裴丞相为淮西节度使以招讨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372103_comment'></div>丞相请公以行。于是以公因本官兼御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372103_comment'></div>赐三品服及鱼。为行军司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372103_comment'></div>从丞相居于郾城。公知蔡州精卒悉聚界上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372103_comment'></div>以拒官军。守城者率老弱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372103_comment'></div>且不过千人。亟白丞相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372103_comment'></div>请以兵三千人间道以入。必擒吴元济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372103_comment'></div>丞相未及行。而李愬自唐州文城垒提其卒以夜入蔡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372103_comment'></div>果得元济。蔡州既平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372103_comment'></div>布衣柏耆以计谒公。公与语奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372103_comment'></div>遂白丞相曰。淮西灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372103_comment'></div>王承宗胆破。可不劳用众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372103_comment'></div>宜使辩士奉相公书。明祸福以招之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372103_comment'></div>彼必服。丞相然之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372103_comment'></div>公令柏耆口占为丞相书。明祸福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372103_comment'></div>使柏耆袖之。以至镇州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372103_comment'></div>承宗果大恐。上表请割德棣二州以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372103_comment'></div>丞相归京师。公迁刑部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372103_comment'></div>岁馀。佛骨自凤翔至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372103_comment'></div>传京师诸寺。时百姓有烧指与顶以祈福者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372103_comment'></div>公奏疏言。自伏羲至周文武时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372103_comment'></div>皆未有佛。而年多至百岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1372103_comment'></div>有过之者。自佛法入中国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1372103_comment'></div>帝王事之。寿不能长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1372103_comment'></div>梁武帝事之最谨。而国大乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1372103_comment'></div>请烧弃佛骨。疏入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1372103_comment'></div>贬潮州刺史。移袁州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1372103_comment'></div>百姓以男女为人隶者。公皆计佣以偿其直而出归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1372103_comment'></div>入迁国子祭酒。有直讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1372103_comment'></div>能说礼而陋于容。学官多豪族子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1372103_comment'></div>摈之不得共食。公命吏曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1372103_comment'></div>召直讲来。与祭酒共食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1372103_comment'></div>学官由此不敢贱直讲。奏儒生为学官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1372103_comment'></div>日使会讲。生徒奔走听闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1372103_comment'></div>皆相喜曰。韩公来为祭酒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1372103_comment'></div>国子监不寂寞矣。改兵部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1372103_comment'></div>镇州乱。杀其帅田宏正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1372103_comment'></div>征之不克。遂以王庭凑为节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1372103_comment'></div>诏公往宣抚。既行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1372103_comment'></div>众皆危之。元稹奏曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1372103_comment'></div>韩愈可惜。穆宗亦悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1372103_comment'></div>有诏令至境观事势。无必于入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1372103_comment'></div>公曰。安有受君命而滞留自顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1372103_comment'></div>遂疾驱入。庭凑严兵拔刃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1372103_comment'></div>弦弓矢以逆。及馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1372103_comment'></div>甲士罗于庭。公与庭凑监军使三人就位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1372103_comment'></div>既坐。庭凑言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1372103_comment'></div>所以纷纷者。乃此士卒所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1372103_comment'></div>本非庭凑心。公大声曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1372103_comment'></div>天子以为尚书有将帅材。故赐之以节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1372103_comment'></div>实不知公共健儿语。未尝及大错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1372103_comment'></div>甲士前奋言曰。先太史为国打朱滔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1372103_comment'></div>滔遂败走。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_103_1372103", 1372103, "Clauses/207/Comments/0")'>血衣</span>皆在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1372103_comment'></div>此军何负朝廷。乃以为贼乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1372103_comment'></div>公告曰。儿郎等且勿语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1372103_comment'></div>听愈言。愈将为儿郎已不记先太史之功与忠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1372103_comment'></div>若犹记得。乃大好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1372103_comment'></div>且为逆与顺。利与病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1372103_comment'></div>不能远引古事。但以天宝来祸福为儿郎等明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1372103_comment'></div>安禄山史思明李希烈梁崇义朱滔朱泚吴元济李师道。复有若子若孙在乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1372103_comment'></div>亦有居官者乎。众皆曰无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1372103_comment'></div>又曰。令公以魏博六州归朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1372103_comment'></div>为节度使。后至中书令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1372103_comment'></div>父子皆授旌节。子与孙虽在童幼者亦为好官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1372103_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_115_1372103", 1372103, "Clauses/230/Comments/0")'>穷富极贵</span>。宠荣耀天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1372103_comment'></div>刘悟李祐皆居大镇。王承元年始十七亦仗节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1372103_comment'></div>此皆三军耳所闻也。众乃曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1372103_comment'></div>田宏正刻此军。故军不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1372103_comment'></div>公曰。然汝三军亦害田令公身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1372103_comment'></div>又残其家矣。复何道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1372103_comment'></div>众乃欢曰。侍郎语是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1372103_comment'></div>庭凑恐众心动。遽麾众散出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1372103_comment'></div>因泣谓公曰。侍郎来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1372103_comment'></div>欲令庭凑何所为。公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1372103_comment'></div>神策六军之将。如牛元翼比者不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1372103_comment'></div>但朝廷顾大体。不可以弃之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1372103_comment'></div>而尚书久围之何也。庭凑曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1372103_comment'></div>即出之。公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1372103_comment'></div>若真耳。则无事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1372103_comment'></div>因与之宴而归。而元翼果出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1372103_comment'></div>乃还。于上前尽奏与庭凑言及三军语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1372103_comment'></div>上大悦曰。卿直向伊如此道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1372103_comment'></div>由是有意欲大用之。王武俊赠太师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1372103_comment'></div>呼太史者。燕赵人语也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1372103_comment'></div>转吏部侍郎。凡令史皆不锁厅出入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1372103_comment'></div>或问公。公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1372103_comment'></div>人所以畏鬼者。以其不能见也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1372103_comment'></div>鬼如可见。则人不畏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1372103_comment'></div>选人不得见令史。故令史势重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1372103_comment'></div>听其出入。则势轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1372103_comment'></div>改京兆尹兼御史大夫。特诏不就御史台谒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1372103_comment'></div>后不得引为例。六军将士皆不敢犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1372103_comment'></div>私相告曰。是尚欲烧佛骨者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1372103_comment'></div>安可忤。故贼盗止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1372103_comment'></div>遇旱。米价不敢上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1372103_comment'></div>李绅为御史中丞。械囚送府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1372103_comment'></div>使以尹杖杖之。公曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1372103_comment'></div>安有此。使归其囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1372103_comment'></div>是时绅方幸。宰相欲去之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1372103_comment'></div>故以台与府不协为请。出绅为江西观察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1372103_comment'></div>以公为兵部侍郎。绅既复留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1372103_comment'></div>公入谢。上曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1372103_comment'></div>卿与李绅争何事。公因自辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1372103_comment'></div>数日复为吏部侍郎。长庆四年得病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1372103_comment'></div>满百日假。既罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1372103_comment'></div>以十二月二日卒于靖安里第。公气厚性通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1372103_comment'></div>论议多大体。与人交始终不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1372103_comment'></div>凡嫁内外及交友之女无主者十人。幼养于嫂郑氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1372103_comment'></div>及嫂殁。为之服期以报之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1372103_comment'></div>深于文章。每以为自扬雄之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1372103_comment'></div>作者不出。其为文未尝效前人之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1372103_comment'></div>而固与之并。自贞元末以至于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1372103_comment'></div>后进之士。其有志于古文者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1372103_comment'></div>莫不视公以为法。有集四十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1372103_comment'></div>小集十卷。及病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1372103_comment'></div>遂请告以罢。每与交友言既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1372103_comment'></div>终以处妻子之语。且曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1372103_comment'></div>某伯兄德行高。晓方药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1372103_comment'></div>食必视本草。年止于四十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1372103_comment'></div>某疏愚。食不择<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_170_1372103", 1372103, "Clauses/341/Comments/0")'>禁忌</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1372103_comment'></div>位为侍郎。年出伯兄十五岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1372103_comment'></div>如又不足。于何而足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1372103_comment'></div>且获终于牖下。幸不至失大节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1372103_comment'></div>以下见先人。可谓荣矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1372103_comment'></div>享年五十七。赠礼部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1372103_comment'></div>谨具任官事迹如前。请牒考功下太常定谥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1372103_comment'></div>并牒史馆。谨状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1372103_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_178_1372103_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript:
