ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=827&endYear=827')">827年</a>　因韦处厚之谏，以本官知制诰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年2月</a>　拜中书舍人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年4月</a>　在中书舍人任，荐谏议大夫柏耆使沧州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年5月</a>　柏耆以擅入沧州擒李同捷得罪贬循州司户，李翱坐谬举左授少府少监。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年6月</a>　有祭韦处厚文。作品：《祭中书韦相公文》<div id='poem_1372108' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372108' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372108?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭中书韦相公文</a><span class='authorDate'>（829年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372108")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372108_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372108'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372108'>呜呼。蕴德在躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372108_comment'></div>必逢其庆。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1372108", 1372108, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>利物</span>之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372108_comment'></div>宜乎得政。君居翰林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372108_comment'></div>遭国之病。建立诏制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372108_comment'></div>所颁未定。决危疑于一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372108_comment'></div>讨篡逆以从正。横兵刃以森列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372108_comment'></div>述王心而革命。伏群情于顷刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372108_comment'></div>咸属目以生敬。既名遂而众安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372108_comment'></div>乃登庸而辅圣。窒因依之他路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372108_comment'></div>收<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1372108", 1372108, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>爵赏</span>之全柄。升俊良之滞淹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372108_comment'></div>摧<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1372108", 1372108, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>奸凶</span>之炽盛。何襮柔而中毅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372108_comment'></div>护勋贤于视听。惟廷相之雍雍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372108_comment'></div>伊近世而畴并。将协德以致理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372108_comment'></div>事有初而未竟。方陈谋于帝前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372108_comment'></div>忽颠仆以终命。虽禀受之有数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372108_comment'></div>亦生灵之不幸。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372108_comment'></div>缅维昔岁。陪迹南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372108_comment'></div>省己何有。辱交于公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372108_comment'></div>公贤偶时。羽若飞鸿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372108_comment'></div>走斥于外。困不能通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372108_comment'></div>公相未几。遽归自东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372108_comment'></div>司谏左垣。视草禁中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372108_comment'></div>汲引之惠。如帆得风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372108_comment'></div>飘沦八年。颠白成翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372108_comment'></div>幽蛰忽发。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1372108", 1372108, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>涣然</span>启蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372108_comment'></div>烈士感知。矧惟贱躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372108_comment'></div>间以存殁。心悲曷穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372108_comment'></div>奠爵而拜。公其表衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372108_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372108_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1372108_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年7月19日</a>　有与白居易同祭故相兴元节度使李绛文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　出为郑州刺史。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='0ed5855b0d2c4d66ace37ab70da3f10d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0ed5855b0d2c4d66ace37ab70da3f10d");'><span id='0ed5855b0d2c4d66ace37ab70da3f10d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>，62岁</div><div id='0ed5855b0d2c4d66ace37ab70da3f10d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>　转户部侍郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年8月</a>　出为襄州刺史、山南东道节度使。<br /></div>

<div class='label1' id='6658e089856a4e4494e2cdb3471672bc_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6658e089856a4e4494e2cdb3471672bc");'><span id='6658e089856a4e4494e2cdb3471672bc_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=796&endYear=796')">796年7月</a>　自徐州至汴州，与时任汴州观察推官的韩愈定交。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=796&endYear=796')">796年</a>　汴州将邓惟恭心怀不轨，汴州司马陆长源白宰相，使汴州人执邓惟恭归于京师，李翱以为陆长源去除乱本，功在天下，作书寄贺。作品：《贺行军陆大夫书》<div id='poem_1372044' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372044' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372044?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺行军陆大夫书</a><span class='authorDate'>（796年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372044")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372044_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372044'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372044'>某月日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372044_comment'></div>布衣李翱寄贺书谨再拜大夫阁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372044_comment'></div>窃闻阁下白宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372044_comment'></div>使汴州人执邓惟恭归于京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372044_comment'></div>奏天子处其轻重生死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372044_comment'></div>伏睹诏书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372044_comment'></div>舍惟恭死罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372044_comment'></div>俾永为黔首于汴州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372044_comment'></div>翱九月时上宰相书言政刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372044_comment'></div>中有词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372044_comment'></div>亲戚怀二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372044_comment'></div>杀之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372044_comment'></div>况怀二且非亲戚哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372044_comment'></div>当是时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372044_comment'></div>惟恭在其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372044_comment'></div>故不直书而微其词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372044_comment'></div>然则惟恭之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372044_comment'></div>闻知于四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372044_comment'></div>其孔甚已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372044_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372044_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1372044", 1372044, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>乱本</span>既除矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372044_comment'></div>自兹日厥后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372044_comment'></div>汴宋颍亳人其无事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372044_comment'></div>岂汴宋颍亳人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372044_comment'></div>实天下皆受其利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372044_comment'></div>昔阁下为建州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372044_comment'></div>人足食与衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372044_comment'></div>且知廉耻礼义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372044_comment'></div>治平为天下第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372044_comment'></div>其为信州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372044_comment'></div>犹建州也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372044_comment'></div>其为汝州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372044_comment'></div>犹信州也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372044_comment'></div>汴人苦其政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372044_comment'></div>失其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372044_comment'></div>十五年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372044_comment'></div>久则不易变矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372044_comment'></div>亦惟阁下孜孜不怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372044_comment'></div>致汴州犹汝州也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372044_comment'></div>天下莫不幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372044_comment'></div>而翱则喜乐乎万世之民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372044_comment'></div>所以然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372044_comment'></div>夫陋巷短褐躬学古知道之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372044_comment'></div>其所以异于朝廷藩翰大臣王公卿士者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372044_comment'></div>口未尝餍乎肥甘尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372044_comment'></div>体未尝焕乎绮纨尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372044_comment'></div>目未尝悦乎采色尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372044_comment'></div>耳未尝乐乎声音尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372044_comment'></div>居处未尝宿乎华屋尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372044_comment'></div>出游未尝乘乎乘黄尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372044_comment'></div>禄利未尝入于家尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372044_comment'></div>名字未尝得进于天王尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372044_comment'></div>其如此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372044_comment'></div>至若忧天下之艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372044_comment'></div>幸天下之和平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372044_comment'></div>乐天下之人民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372044_comment'></div>得与其身臻乎仁寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372044_comment'></div>思九夷八蛮解辫发椎髻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372044_comment'></div>同车书文轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372044_comment'></div>则虽朝廷藩翰大臣王公卿士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372044_comment'></div>亦未必皆甚乎陋巷短褐躬学古知道之人者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372044_comment'></div>若必皆甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372044_comment'></div>则天下之理得日变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372044_comment'></div>可以如响之应乎声也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372044_comment'></div>故天地山川草木鳞羽之瑞有一可以为升平之符者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372044_comment'></div>时政有一可以教民者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372044_comment'></div>藩屏之臣有一可以长人行化者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372044_comment'></div>则未尝不私自喜乐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372044_comment'></div>万类含育有一伤和平之气者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372044_comment'></div>夷狄蛮戎之俗有一咈乎道者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372044_comment'></div>时政有一不毗于下民者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372044_comment'></div>则未尝不私自忧惧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372044_comment'></div>而况其远者大者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1372044_comment'></div>天下之一善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1372044_comment'></div>故不足以喜乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1372044_comment'></div>然多其善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1372044_comment'></div>则太平之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1372044_comment'></div>可庶几乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1372044_comment'></div>天下之一不善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1372044_comment'></div>故不足以忧惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1372044_comment'></div>然累其不善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1372044_comment'></div>则颠覆之形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1372044_comment'></div>殆将至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1372044_comment'></div>太平之基。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1372044_comment'></div>颠覆之形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1372044_comment'></div>乃从政者之所喜乐忧惧尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1372044_comment'></div>其为布衣守道之人不同任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1372044_comment'></div>如耳之不司采色文章也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1372044_comment'></div>而与知之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1372044_comment'></div>士之躬学古知道者。<div class='inline' /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在汴州，韩愈为其言高愍女事，李翱作文纪之。作品：《高愍女碑》<div id='poem_1372088' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372088' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372088?labeling=true' target='_blank'>高悯女碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（797年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1372088'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372088'>悯女姓高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372088_comment'></div>妹妹名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372088_comment'></div>生七岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372088_comment'></div>当建中二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372088_comment'></div>父彦昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372088_comment'></div>以濮阳归天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372088_comment'></div>前此逆贼质妹妹与其母兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372088_comment'></div>而使彦昭守濮阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372088_comment'></div>及彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372088_comment'></div>昭以城归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372088_comment'></div>妹妹与其母兄皆死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372088_comment'></div>其母李氏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372088_comment'></div>将死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372088_comment'></div>怜妹妹之幼无辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372088_comment'></div>请独免其死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372088_comment'></div>而以为婢于官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372088_comment'></div>众皆许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372088_comment'></div>妹妹不欲曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372088_comment'></div>生而受辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372088_comment'></div>不如死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372088_comment'></div>母兄且皆不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372088_comment'></div>何独生为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372088_comment'></div>其母与兄将被刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372088_comment'></div>咸拜于四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372088_comment'></div>妹妹独曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372088_comment'></div>我家为忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372088_comment'></div>宗党诛夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372088_comment'></div>四方神祗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372088_comment'></div>尚何知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372088_comment'></div>问其父所在之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372088_comment'></div>西向哭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372088_comment'></div>再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372088_comment'></div>遂就死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372088_comment'></div>明年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372088_comment'></div>太常谥之曰悯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372088_comment'></div>当此之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372088_comment'></div>天下之为父母者闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372088_comment'></div>莫不欲悯女之为其子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372088_comment'></div>天下之为夫者闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372088_comment'></div>莫不欲悯女之为其室家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372088_comment'></div>天下之为女与妻者闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372088_comment'></div>莫不欲悯女之行在其身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372088_comment'></div>昔者曹娥思盱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372088_comment'></div>自沉于江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372088_comment'></div>狱吏嘑囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372088_comment'></div>章女悲号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372088_comment'></div>思唁其兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372088_comment'></div>作诗载驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372088_comment'></div>缇萦上书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372088_comment'></div>乃除肉刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372088_comment'></div>彼四女者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372088_comment'></div>或孝或智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372088_comment'></div>或义或仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372088_comment'></div>噫此悯女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372088_comment'></div>厥生七岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372088_comment'></div>天生其知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372088_comment'></div>四女不伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372088_comment'></div>向遂推而布之于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372088_comment'></div>其谁不从而化焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372088_comment'></div>虽有逆子必改行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372088_comment'></div>虽有悍妻必易心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372088_comment'></div>赏一女而天下劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372088_comment'></div>亦王化之大端也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372088_comment'></div>异哉悯女之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372088_comment'></div>而不家闻户知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372088_comment'></div>贞元十三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372088_comment'></div>翱在汴州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372088_comment'></div>彦昭时为颍州剌史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372088_comment'></div>昌黎韩愈始为余言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372088_comment'></div>余既悲而嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372088_comment'></div>于是作高悯女碑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_70_1372088_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在汴州，有文。作品：《杨烈妇传》<div id='poem_1372105' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372105' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372105?labeling=true' target='_blank'>杨烈妇传</a><span class='authorDate'>（797年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372105")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372105_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372105'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372105'>建中四年。李希烈陷汴州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372105_comment'></div>既又将盗陈州。分其兵数千人抵项城县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372105_comment'></div>盖将掠其玉帛。俘累其男女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372105_comment'></div>以会于陈州。县令李侃不知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372105_comment'></div>其妻杨氏曰。君县令也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372105_comment'></div>寇至当守。力不足死焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372105_comment'></div>职也。君如逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372105_comment'></div>则谁守。侃曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372105_comment'></div>兵与财皆无。将若何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372105_comment'></div>杨氏曰。如不守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372105_comment'></div>县为贼所得矣。仓廪皆其积也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372105_comment'></div>府库皆其财也。百姓皆其战士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372105_comment'></div>国家何有。夺贼之财而食其食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372105_comment'></div>重赏以令死士。其必济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372105_comment'></div>于是召胥吏百姓于庭。杨氏言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372105_comment'></div>县令诚主也。虽然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372105_comment'></div>岁满则罢去。非若吏人百姓然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372105_comment'></div>吏人百姓。邑人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372105_comment'></div>坟墓存焉。宜相与致死以守其邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372105_comment'></div>忍失其身而为贼之人耶。众皆泣许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372105_comment'></div>乃徇曰。以瓦石中贼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372105_comment'></div>与之千钱。以刀矢兵刃之物中贼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372105_comment'></div>与之万钱。得数百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372105_comment'></div>侃率之以乘城。杨氏亲为之爨以食之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372105_comment'></div>无长少。必周而均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372105_comment'></div>使侃与贼言曰。项城父老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372105_comment'></div>义不为贼矣。皆悉力守死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372105_comment'></div>得吾城。不足以威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372105_comment'></div>不如亟去。徒失利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372105_comment'></div>无益也。贼皆笑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372105_comment'></div>有蜚箭集于侃之手。伤而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372105_comment'></div>杨氏责之曰。君不在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372105_comment'></div>则人谁肯固矣。与其死于城上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372105_comment'></div>不犹愈于家乎。侃遂忍之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372105_comment'></div>复登陴。项城小邑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372105_comment'></div>无长戟劲弩高城深沟之固。贼气吞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372105_comment'></div>率其徒将超城而下。有以弱弓射贼者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372105_comment'></div>中其帅坠马死。其帅希烈之婿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372105_comment'></div>贼失势。遂相与散走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372105_comment'></div>项城之人无伤焉。剌史上侃之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372105_comment'></div>诏迁绛州太平县令。杨氏至兹犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372105_comment'></div>妇人女子之德。奉父母舅姑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372105_comment'></div>尽恭顺。和于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1372105", 1372105, "Clauses/85/Comments/0")'>娣姒</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372105_comment'></div>于卑幼有慈爱。而能不失其贞者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372105_comment'></div>则贤矣。至于辨行阵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372105_comment'></div>明攻守勇烈之道。此固公卿大臣之所难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372105_comment'></div>厥自兵兴。朝廷注意<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1372105", 1372105, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>宠旌</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372105_comment'></div>守御之臣。凭坚城深池之险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372105_comment'></div>储蓄山积。货财自若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372105_comment'></div>冠冑服甲。负弓矢而驰者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372105_comment'></div>不知几人。其勇不能战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372105_comment'></div>其智不能守。其忠不能死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372105_comment'></div>弃其城而走者有矣。彼何人哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372105_comment'></div>若杨氏者。妇人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372105_comment'></div>孔子曰。仁者必有勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372105_comment'></div>杨氏当之矣。赞曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372105_comment'></div>凡人之情。皆谓后来者不及于古之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372105_comment'></div>贤者自古亦稀。独后代耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372105_comment'></div>及其有之。与古人不殊也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372105_comment'></div>若高悯女杨烈妇者。虽古烈女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372105_comment'></div>其何加焉。予惧其行事堙灭而不传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372105_comment'></div>故皆叙之。将告于史官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372105_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1372105_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='dd7cee2426474f8e82bb31d68267d873_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dd7cee2426474f8e82bb31d68267d873");'><span id='dd7cee2426474f8e82bb31d68267d873_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=799&endYear=799')">799年</a>，26岁</div><div id='dd7cee2426474f8e82bb31d68267d873' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=799&endYear=799')">799年</a>　早春，在汴州，孟郊自汴南归，李翱与韩愈、孟郊等联句，未几，亦去汴南游。作品：《远游联句》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='701f9332108944eea0f331565ffcfb06_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("701f9332108944eea0f331565ffcfb06");'><span id='701f9332108944eea0f331565ffcfb06_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年</a>，28岁</div><div id='701f9332108944eea0f331565ffcfb06' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年9月8日</a>　在汴州，葬祖父李楚金于陈留安丰乡。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a6ba97940cea43e0a35d762ec01aa7bf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a6ba97940cea43e0a35d762ec01aa7bf");'><span id='a6ba97940cea43e0a35d762ec01aa7bf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=803&endYear=803')">803年</a>，30岁</div><div id='a6ba97940cea43e0a35d762ec01aa7bf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=803&endYear=803')">803年1月</a>　葬妻韦你于陈留安丰乡冈原并作墓志。作品：《故朔方节度掌书记殿中侍御史昌黎韩君夫人京兆韦氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1372101' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372101' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372101?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故朔方节度掌书记殿中侍御史昌黎韩君夫人京兆韦氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（803年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372101")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372101_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372101'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372101'>夫人姓京兆韦氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372101_comment'></div>尚舍奉御说之次女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372101_comment'></div>年十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372101_comment'></div>执妇道于昌黎韩氏府君讳弇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372101_comment'></div>自后魏尚书令安定桓王六世生礼部郎中云卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372101_comment'></div>礼部实生府君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372101_comment'></div>进士及第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372101_comment'></div>朔方节度请掌书记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372101_comment'></div>得秘书省校书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372101_comment'></div>累迁殿中侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372101_comment'></div>贞元三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372101_comment'></div>吐蕃乞盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372101_comment'></div>诏朔方节度使即塞上与之盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372101_comment'></div>宾客皆从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372101_comment'></div>其五月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372101_comment'></div>吐蕃不肯盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372101_comment'></div>殿中君于是遇害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372101_comment'></div>时年三十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372101_comment'></div>夫人始年十有七矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372101_comment'></div>有女子一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372101_comment'></div>其生七月而孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372101_comment'></div>夫人之母前既不幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372101_comment'></div>夫人以其女子归于其父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372101_comment'></div>弗数年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372101_comment'></div>其父又不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372101_comment'></div>夫人泣血食贫养其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372101_comment'></div>有道自慎于嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372101_comment'></div>节行愈高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372101_comment'></div>虽烈丈夫之志不如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372101_comment'></div>犹有董氏姊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372101_comment'></div>继衣食仁之焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372101_comment'></div>不数年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372101_comment'></div>董氏姊又不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372101_comment'></div>夫人于是天下无所归托矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372101_comment'></div>殿中君从父弟愈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372101_comment'></div>孝友慈祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372101_comment'></div>贞元十六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372101_comment'></div>以其女子归于陇西李翱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372101_comment'></div>夫人从其女子依于李氏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372101_comment'></div>降年短命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372101_comment'></div>三十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372101_comment'></div>贞元十八年八月甲辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372101_comment'></div>卒于汴州开封新里乡之某村。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372101_comment'></div>其明年正月辛酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372101_comment'></div>陇西李氏以其丧葬之于陈留县安丰乡冈原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372101_comment'></div>殿中君之先葬于河阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372101_comment'></div>惟君之没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372101_comment'></div>不得其丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372101_comment'></div>夫人是以不克葬于河阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372101_comment'></div>而独坟于陈留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372101_comment'></div>弗克祔于殿中君之族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372101_comment'></div>而依于女子氏之党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372101_comment'></div>以从女子之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372101_comment'></div>权道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372101_comment'></div>且将有待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372101_comment'></div>殿中君文行甚修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372101_comment'></div>位甚卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372101_comment'></div>没于王事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372101_comment'></div>初礼部君好立节义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372101_comment'></div>有大功于昭陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372101_comment'></div>其文章出于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372101_comment'></div>而官不甚高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372101_comment'></div>殿中君又无嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372101_comment'></div>尝闻诸君子曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372101_comment'></div>位不称德者有后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372101_comment'></div>礼部君曷为然哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372101_comment'></div>于是叙其孤女之悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372101_comment'></div>以志于墓门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372101_comment'></div>铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372101_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_1372101'>女子之生兮七月而孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372101_comment'></div>所恃者母兮夫何辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372101_comment'></div>天苍苍兮不回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372101_comment'></div>生几时兮终日哀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_72_1372101_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5709fcd931ae4d84b674baa8d7096fd8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5709fcd931ae4d84b674baa8d7096fd8");'><span id='5709fcd931ae4d84b674baa8d7096fd8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年</a>，36岁</div><div id='5709fcd931ae4d84b674baa8d7096fd8' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年1月28日</a>　南行途中，次汴州，疾加剧召医察脉。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年2月1日</a>　南行途中，宿陈留。<br /></div>

id='poem_sentence_2_30343_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=812&endYear=812')">812年</a>　在浙东幕，有书答考功员外郎知制诰独孤郁。作品：《答独孤舍人书》<div id='poem_1372033' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372033' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372033?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答独孤舍人书</a><span class='authorDate'>（812年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372033")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372033_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372033'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372033'>足下书中有无怨怼以至疏索之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372033_comment'></div>盖是戏言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372033_comment'></div>然亦似未相悉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372033_comment'></div>荐贤进能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372033_comment'></div>自是足下公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372033_comment'></div>如不为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372033_comment'></div>亦自是足下所阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372033_comment'></div>在仆何苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372033_comment'></div>乃至怨怼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372033_comment'></div>仆尝怪董生大贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372033_comment'></div>而著士不遇赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372033_comment'></div>惜其自待不厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372033_comment'></div>凡人之蓄道德才智于身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372033_comment'></div>以待时用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372033_comment'></div>盖将以代天理物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372033_comment'></div>非为衣服饮食之鲜肥而为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372033_comment'></div>董生道德备具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372033_comment'></div>武帝不用为相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372033_comment'></div>故汉德不如三代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372033_comment'></div>而生人受其憔悴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372033_comment'></div>于董生何苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372033_comment'></div>而为士不遇之词乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372033_comment'></div>仆意绪间自待甚厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372033_comment'></div>此身穷达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372033_comment'></div>岂关仆之贵贱耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372033_comment'></div>虽终身如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372033_comment'></div>固无恨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372033_comment'></div>况年犹未甚老哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372033_comment'></div>去年足下有相引荐意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372033_comment'></div>当时恐有所累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372033_comment'></div>犹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1372033", 1372033, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>奉止</span>不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372033_comment'></div>何遽不相悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372033_comment'></div>所以不数附书者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372033_comment'></div>一二年来往还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372033_comment'></div>多得官在京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372033_comment'></div>既不能周遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372033_comment'></div>又且无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372033_comment'></div>性颇慵懒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372033_comment'></div>便一切<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_38_1372033", 1372033, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>画断</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372033_comment'></div>祇作报书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372033_comment'></div>又以为苟相知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372033_comment'></div>固不在书之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1372033", 1372033, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>疏数</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372033_comment'></div>如不相知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372033_comment'></div>尚何求而数书哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372033_comment'></div>惟往还中有贫贱更不如仆者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372033_comment'></div>即数数附书耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372033_comment'></div>近频得人书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372033_comment'></div>皆责疏简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372033_comment'></div>故具之于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372033_comment'></div>见相怪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372033_comment'></div>当为辞焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1372033_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=813&endYear=813')">813年</a>　在浙东幕，有书答皇甫湜言及其欲著唐史。作品：《答皇甫湜书》<div id='poem_1372034' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372034' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372034?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答皇甫湜书</a><span class='authorDate'>（813年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372034")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372034_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372034'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372034'>辱书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372034_comment'></div>览所寄文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372034_comment'></div>词高理直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372034_comment'></div>欢悦无量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372034_comment'></div>有足发予者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372034_comment'></div>自别足下来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372034_comment'></div>仆口不曾言文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372034_comment'></div>非不好也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372034_comment'></div>言无所益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372034_comment'></div>众亦未信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372034_comment'></div>祇足以招谤忤物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372034_comment'></div>于道无明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372034_comment'></div>故不言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372034_comment'></div>仆到越中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372034_comment'></div>得一官三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372034_comment'></div>材能甚薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372034_comment'></div>泽不被物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372034_comment'></div>月费官钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372034_comment'></div>自度终无补益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372034_comment'></div>屡求罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372034_comment'></div>尚未得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372034_comment'></div>以为愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372034_comment'></div>仆性不解谄佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372034_comment'></div>生不能曲事权贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372034_comment'></div>以故不得齿于朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372034_comment'></div>而足下亦抱屈在外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372034_comment'></div>故略有所说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372034_comment'></div>凡古贤圣得位于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372034_comment'></div>道行天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372034_comment'></div>皆不著书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372034_comment'></div>以其事业存于制度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372034_comment'></div>足以自见故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372034_comment'></div>其著书者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372034_comment'></div>盖道德充积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372034_comment'></div>阨摧于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372034_comment'></div>身卑处下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372034_comment'></div>泽不能润物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372034_comment'></div>耻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1372034", 1372034, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>灰泯</span>而烬灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372034_comment'></div>又无圣人为之发明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372034_comment'></div>故假空言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372034_comment'></div>是非一代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372034_comment'></div>以传无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372034_comment'></div>而自光耀于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372034_comment'></div>故或往往有著书者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372034_comment'></div>仆近写得唐书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372034_comment'></div>史官才薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372034_comment'></div>言词鄙浅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372034_comment'></div>不足以发明高祖太宗列圣明德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372034_comment'></div>使后之观者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372034_comment'></div>文采不及周汉之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372034_comment'></div>仆以为西汉十一帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372034_comment'></div>高祖起布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372034_comment'></div>定天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372034_comment'></div>豁达大度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372034_comment'></div>东汉所不及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372034_comment'></div>其馀惟文宣二帝为优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372034_comment'></div>自惠景以下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372034_comment'></div>亦不皆明于东汉明章两帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372034_comment'></div>而前汉事迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372034_comment'></div>灼然传在人口者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372034_comment'></div>以司马迁班固叙述高简之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372034_comment'></div>故学者悦而习焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372034_comment'></div>其读之详也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372034_comment'></div>足下读范蔚宗汉书陈寿三国志王隐晋书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372034_comment'></div>生熟何如左邱明司马迁班固书之温习哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372034_comment'></div>故温习者事迹彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372034_comment'></div>而罕读者事迹晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372034_comment'></div>读之疏数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372034_comment'></div>在词之高下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372034_comment'></div>理之必然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372034_comment'></div>唐有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372034_comment'></div>圣明继于周汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372034_comment'></div>而史官叙事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1372034_comment'></div>曾不如范蔚宗陈寿所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1372034_comment'></div>况足拟望左邱明司马迁班固之文哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1372034_comment'></div>仆所以为耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1372034_comment'></div>当兹得于时者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1372034_comment'></div>虽负作者之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1372034_comment'></div>其道既能被物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1372034_comment'></div>则不肯著书矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1372034_comment'></div>仆窃不自度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1372034_comment'></div>无位于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1372034_comment'></div>幸有馀暇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1372034_comment'></div>而词句足以称赞明盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1372034_comment'></div>纪一代功臣贤士行迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1372034_comment'></div>灼然可传于后代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1372034_comment'></div>自以为能不灭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1372034_comment'></div>不敢为让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1372034_comment'></div>故欲笔削国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1372034_comment'></div>成不刊之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1372034_comment'></div>用仲尼褒贬之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1372034_comment'></div>取天下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_91_1372034", 1372034, "Clauses/91/Comments/0")'>公是公非</span>以为本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1372034_comment'></div>群党之所谓为是者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1372034_comment'></div>仆未必以为是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1372034_comment'></div>群党之所谓为非者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1372034_comment'></div>仆未必以为非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1372034_comment'></div>使仆书成而传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1372034_comment'></div>则富贵而功德不著者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1372034_comment'></div>未必声名于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1372034_comment'></div>贫贱而道德全者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1372034_comment'></div>未必不烜赫于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1372034_comment'></div>韩退之所谓诛奸谀于既死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1372034_comment'></div>发潜德之幽光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1372034_comment'></div>是翱心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1372034_comment'></div>仆文采虽不足以希左邱明司马子长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1372034_comment'></div>足下视仆叙高悯女杨烈妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1372034_comment'></div>岂尽出班孟坚蔡伯喈之下耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1372034_comment'></div>仲尼有言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1372034_comment'></div>不有博弈者乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1372034_comment'></div>为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1372034_comment'></div>犹贤乎已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1372034_comment'></div>仆所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1372034_comment'></div>虽无益于人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1372034_comment'></div>比之博弈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1372034_comment'></div>犹为胜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1372034_comment'></div>足下以为何如哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1372034_comment'></div>古之贤圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1372034_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_117_1372034", 1372034, "Clauses/117/Comments/0")'>当仁不让</span>于师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1372034_comment'></div>仲尼则曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1372034_comment'></div>文王既没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1372034_comment'></div>文不在兹乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1372034_comment'></div>又曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1372034_comment'></div>子欲无言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1372034_comment'></div>天何言哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1372034_comment'></div>孟子则曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1372034_comment'></div>吾之不遇鲁侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1372034_comment'></div>天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1372034_comment'></div>臧氏之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1372034_comment'></div>安能使予不遇乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1372034_comment'></div>司马迁则曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1372034_comment'></div>成一家之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1372034_comment'></div>藏之名山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1372034_comment'></div>以俟后圣人君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1372034_comment'></div>仆之不让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1372034_comment'></div>亦非大过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1372034_comment'></div>幸无怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1372034_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_136_1372034_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=814&endYear=814')">814年1月</a>　在浙东幕，改葬叔父李术，作墓志铭。作品：《叔氏墓志铭》<div id='poem_1372094' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372094' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372094?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叔氏墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（814年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372094")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372094_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372094'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372094'>元和九年岁直甲午正月十九日丁卯，浙东道观察判官将仕郎试大理评事摄监察御史李翱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372094_comment'></div>奉其叔氏之丧葬于兹，叔氏讳术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372094_comment'></div>生子曰王老，远在京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372094_comment'></div>翱实主其事，铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372094_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1372094'>翱生始言，叔氏弃殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372094_comment'></div>爰殡于野，年周四甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372094_comment'></div>岂无诸亲，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1372094", 1372094, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>生故</span>或迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372094_comment'></div>亦有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1372094", 1372094, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>息子</span>，旅宦京国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372094_comment'></div>邱坟孰封，松槚未列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372094_comment'></div>殡宇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1372094", 1372094, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>零毁</span>，狐狸所穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372094_comment'></div>中夜远思，酸悽心骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372094_comment'></div>是以乞假公府，言来筮宅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372094_comment'></div>追念延陵，丧子嬴博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372094_comment'></div>葬不归吴，于礼其合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372094_comment'></div>唯叔平生，游居是邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372094_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1372094", 1372094, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>夭谢</span>于此，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1372094", 1372094, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>灵幽</span>其托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372094_comment'></div>女侄之西，仲兄之北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372094_comment'></div>冥昭何异，可用<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1372094", 1372094, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>居息</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372094_comment'></div>孰为故乡，乃树松柏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372094_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1372094_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=814&endYear=814')">814年</a>　在浙东幕，元和八九年间，撰侯高墓志。作品：《故处士侯君墓志》<div id='poem_1372099' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372099' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372099?labeling=true' target='_blank'>故处士侯君墓志</a><span class='authorDate'>（814年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372099")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372099_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372099'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372099'>侯高字元览。上谷人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372099_comment'></div>少为道士。学黄老练气保形之术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372099_comment'></div>居庐山。号华阳居士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372099_comment'></div>每激发则为文达意。其高处<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1372099", 1372099, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>骎骎</span>乎有汉魏之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372099_comment'></div>性刚劲。怀救物之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372099_comment'></div>自侪周昌王陵。所如固不合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372099_comment'></div>视贵善宦者如粪溲。与平昌孟郊东野昌黎韩愈退之陇西李渤浚之河南独孤朗用晦陇西李翱习之相往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372099_comment'></div>汴州乱。兵士杀留后陆长源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372099_comment'></div>东取刘逸淮。乃作吊汴州文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372099_comment'></div>投之大川以诉。贞元十五年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372099_comment'></div>翱遇元览于苏州。出其词以示翱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372099_comment'></div>翱谓孟东野曰。诚之至者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372099_comment'></div>必上通上帝闻之。刘逸淮其将不久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372099_comment'></div>后数月而刘逸淮竟死。其首章曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372099_comment'></div>穹穹与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1372099", 1372099, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>厚厚</span>兮。乌愤予而不摅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372099_comment'></div>翱以为与屈原宋玉景差相上下。自东方朔严忌皆不及也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372099_comment'></div>达奚抚为楚州。起摄盱眙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372099_comment'></div>祭酒李公逊刺衢州。请治信安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372099_comment'></div>其观察浙东。又宰于剡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372099_comment'></div>三县皆有政。不幸得心疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372099_comment'></div>留其子狗儿于翱家而归庐山。不到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372099_comment'></div>卒江西。其子婿王适使佣吉勉求君所如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372099_comment'></div>值君卒。吉勉以君丧殡于袁州之野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372099_comment'></div>而复于适。适又死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372099_comment'></div>适之妻使吉勉来告于翱。翱以狗儿归适妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372099_comment'></div>居二年。适妻又死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372099_comment'></div>狗儿尚童。翱虑吉勉之短长不可期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372099_comment'></div>则君之丧终不坟矣。故使吉勉往葬之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372099_comment'></div>而识其墓。以示狗儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372099_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1372099_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=814&endYear=814')">814年9月</a>　李逊入朝为给事中，李翱或于是时或稍后罢任。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
泗县
-----detail

showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372048?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答泗州开元寺僧澄观书</a><span class='authorDate'>（799年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372048")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372048'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372048'>前日见命作开元寺钟铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372048_comment'></div>云欲藉仆之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372048_comment'></div>庶几不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372048_comment'></div>而传于后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372048_comment'></div>诚足下相知之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372048_comment'></div>无不到也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372048_comment'></div>虽然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372048_comment'></div>翱学圣人之心焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372048_comment'></div>则不敢让乎知圣人之道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372048_comment'></div>当见命时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372048_comment'></div>意亦思之熟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372048_comment'></div>吾之铭是钟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372048_comment'></div>吾将明圣人之道焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372048_comment'></div>则于释氏无益也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372048_comment'></div>吾将顺释氏之教而述焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372048_comment'></div>则惑乎天下甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372048_comment'></div>何贵乎吾之先觉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372048_comment'></div>吾之词必传于后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372048_comment'></div>后有圣人如仲尼者之读吾词也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372048_comment'></div>则将大责于吾矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372048_comment'></div>吾畏圣人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372048_comment'></div>夫铭古多有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372048_comment'></div>汤之盘铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372048_comment'></div>其词云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372048_comment'></div>卫孔悝之鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372048_comment'></div>其词云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372048_comment'></div>秦始皇之峄山碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372048_comment'></div>其词云云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372048_comment'></div>皆可以纪功伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372048_comment'></div>垂诫劝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372048_comment'></div>铭于盘则曰盘铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372048_comment'></div>于鼎则曰鼎铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372048_comment'></div>于山则曰山铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372048_comment'></div>盘之词可迁于鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372048_comment'></div>鼎之词可迁于山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372048_comment'></div>山之词可迁于碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372048_comment'></div>唯时之所纪耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372048_comment'></div>及蔡邕黄钺铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372048_comment'></div>以纪功于黄钺之上尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372048_comment'></div>或盘或鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372048_comment'></div>或峄山或黄钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372048_comment'></div>其立意与言皆同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372048_comment'></div>非如高唐上林长杨之作赋云尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372048_comment'></div>近代之文士则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372048_comment'></div>为铭为碑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372048_comment'></div>大抵咏其形容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372048_comment'></div>有异于古人之所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372048_comment'></div>其作钟铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372048_comment'></div>则必咏其形容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372048_comment'></div>与其声音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372048_comment'></div>与其财用之多少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372048_comment'></div>镕铸之勤劳尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372048_comment'></div>非所谓勒功德诫劝于器也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372048_comment'></div>推此类而承观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372048_comment'></div>某不知君子之文也亦甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372048_comment'></div>然所为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372048_comment'></div>亦皆有盛名于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372048_comment'></div>天下之人咸谓之善焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372048_comment'></div>吾不知吾所独知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372048_comment'></div>其能贤于他人之皆不知乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372048_comment'></div>天下人咸以不知者云善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372048_comment'></div>则吾之独知又何能云善乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372048_comment'></div>虽然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372048_comment'></div>吾当亦顺吾心以顺圣人尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372048_comment'></div>阿俗从时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372048_comment'></div>则不忍为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372048_comment'></div>故当时甚未敢承教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372048_comment'></div>为其所怀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372048_comment'></div>如前所云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372048_comment'></div>足下欲吾之必铭是钟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372048_comment'></div>当顺吾心与吾道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372048_comment'></div>则足下之铭必传于后代矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372048_comment'></div>如欲从俗之所云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1372048_comment'></div>则天下属词之士愿为之者甚众矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1372048_comment'></div>何藉于李翱之词哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1372048_comment'></div>幸思之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1372048_comment'></div>日中时过淮而南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1372048_comment'></div>书以通意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1372048_comment'></div>且为别。</div><div id='poem_sentence_78_1372048_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='48728fd50e2445d3ac445cb193681c98_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("48728fd50e2445d3ac445cb193681c98");'><span id='48728fd50e2445d3ac445cb193681c98_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年</a>，36岁</div><div id='48728fd50e2445d3ac445cb193681c98' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年2月10日</a>　南行途中，次泗州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
徐州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='42e538409b6a4a1ca7dc0b149b2000fa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("42e538409b6a4a1ca7dc0b149b2000fa");'><span id='42e538409b6a4a1ca7dc0b149b2000fa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年</a>，27岁</div><div id='42e538409b6a4a1ca7dc0b149b2000fa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年</a>　至徐州，有书致时任徐州节度推官的韩愈，劝其入京求进，韩愈有书答之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=800&endYear=800')">800年4月</a>　在徐州，娶韩愈从兄弇之女。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
滑县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='6b2d5c8a5e6f4c5ea630b91e0ec078c2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6b2d5c8a5e6f4c5ea630b91e0ec078c2");'><span id='6b2d5c8a5e6f4c5ea630b91e0ec078c2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=802')">801-802年</a>，28-29岁</div><div id='6b2d5c8a5e6f4c5ea630b91e0ec078c2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年</a>　此前或后一二年，曾为滑州观察使判官，有代滑州节度使李元素作进画马屏风状。作品：《代李尚书进画马屏风状》<div id='poem_1372030' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372030' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372030?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代李尚书进画马屏风状</a><span class='authorDate'>（801年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372030")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372030_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372030'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372030'>右。臣近得前件马样。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372030_comment'></div>以其图写。诸家稍殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372030_comment'></div>试为短屏。备以文采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372030_comment'></div>观其体闲色浮。气逸神骏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372030_comment'></div>练影吴浦。指山川而不摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372030_comment'></div>花攒上林。若雨露之新洗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372030_comment'></div>或屈膝千里。或长鸣九霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372030_comment'></div>昔以负图为宝。今愿捍蔽成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372030_comment'></div>形影不殊。效用何别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372030_comment'></div>谨裁成十二扇。随状奉进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372030_comment'></div>若以时从启闭。犹足靖于尘埃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372030_comment'></div>倘将用以驰驱。庶可效其筋力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372030_comment'></div>辄敢轻冒。战惧伏深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372030_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1372030_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=801&endYear=801')">801年</a>　赠裴度新作二十篇并附书劝其时干进。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=802&endYear=802')">802年</a>　或在滑州任观察判官，祠部员外郎陆傪赴任歙州途中卒于洛阳，李翱作传。作品：《陆歙州述》<div id='poem_1372083' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372083' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372083?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陆歙州述</a><span class='authorDate'>（802年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372083")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372083_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372083'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372083'>吾郡陆傪。字公佐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372083_comment'></div>生于世五十有七年矣。明于仁义之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372083_comment'></div>可以化人伦厚风俗者馀三十年。连事观察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372083_comment'></div>观察使不能知。退居于田者六七年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372083_comment'></div>由侍御史入为祠部员外郎。二年出剌歙州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372083_comment'></div>卒于道。贞元十八年四月二十八日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372083_comment'></div>凡人所不能穷者。必推之于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372083_comment'></div>天之注膏雨也。人心以为生旱苗然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372083_comment'></div>雨与苗运相违。或雨于海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372083_comment'></div>或雨于山。旱苗不得仰其泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372083_comment'></div>惟人也亦然。天之生俊贤也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372083_comment'></div>人之心以为拯憔悴之人然也。贤者与憔悴之人时不合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372083_comment'></div>或死于野。或得其位而道不能行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372083_comment'></div>憔悴之人不得被其惠。膏雨之降也适然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372083_comment'></div>贤者之生于时也亦然。运相合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372083_comment'></div>旱苗仰其泽。憔悴之人赖其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372083_comment'></div>傅说甘盘尹吉甫管夷吾之类也。时勿合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372083_comment'></div>膏雨降虽终日。贤哲生虽比肩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372083_comment'></div>旱苗之不救。百姓之弗赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372083_comment'></div>颜子子思孟子董仲舒之类也。故贤哲之生自有时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372083_comment'></div>百姓之赖其力天也。不赖其力亦天也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372083_comment'></div>呜呼。公佐之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372083_comment'></div>虽升于朝。剌于州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372083_comment'></div>其出入始二年。道之不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372083_comment'></div>与居于田时弗差也。公佐之贤虽日闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372083_comment'></div>其德行未必昭昭然闻于天子。公佐是以不得其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372083_comment'></div>出剌一州。又短命道病死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372083_comment'></div>天下之未蒙其德固宜矣。然则天之生君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372083_comment'></div>授之以救人之道。不授之以救人之位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372083_comment'></div>如膏雨之或雨于海。或雨于山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372083_comment'></div>旱苗之不沐其泽者均也。故君子不得其位以行其道者命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372083_comment'></div>其亦有不足于心者耶。得其道者穷居于野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372083_comment'></div>非所谓屈。冠冕而相天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372083_comment'></div>非所谓伸。其何有不足于心者耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372083_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1372083_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=802&endYear=802')">802年</a>　或在滑州任观察判官。作品：《复性书》<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洛阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='f65aa8e2d5ee4d16aade6d4fb5d51c54_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f65aa8e2d5ee4d16aade6d4fb5d51c54");'><span id='f65aa8e2d5ee4d16aade6d4fb5d51c54_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=809')">806-809年</a>，33-36岁</div><div id='f65aa8e2d5ee4d16aade6d4fb5d51c54' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年4月</a>　寓居洛阳，为岭南节度使徐申作行状。作品：《唐故金紫光禄大夫检校礼部尚书使持节都督广州诸军事兼广州刺史兼御史大夫充岭南节度营田观察制置本管经略等使东海郡开国公食邑二千户徐公行状》<div id='poem_1372102' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372102?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故金紫光禄大夫检校礼部尚书使持节都督广州诸军事兼广州刺史兼御史大夫充岭南节度营田观察制置本管经略等使东海郡开国公食邑二千户徐公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（806年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372102")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372102_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372102'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372102'>曾祖仁彻。隋吉州太和县丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372102_comment'></div>祖元之。皇考功员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372102_comment'></div>赠吏部郎中谏议大夫。考义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372102_comment'></div>皇汾州司户参军。赠信州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372102_comment'></div>京兆府万年县青盖乡交原里东海徐公。年七十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372102_comment'></div>公讳申。字维降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372102_comment'></div>东海剡人。永泰元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372102_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1372102", 1372102, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>寄籍</span>京兆府。举进士秘书省正字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372102_comment'></div>初辟巡官于江西。又掌书记于岭南行营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372102_comment'></div>哥舒氏之乱平。奏授大理寺评事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372102_comment'></div>转司直兼监察御史。赐绯鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372102_comment'></div>又充节度判官于朔方。改太子司议郎兼殿中侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372102_comment'></div>选授洪州都督府长史。时刺史嗣曹王举江西兵讨李希烈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372102_comment'></div>故以长史行刺史事。任职有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372102_comment'></div>曹王荐之。迁韶州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372102_comment'></div>四十馀年刺史相循居于县城。州城与公田三百顷皆为墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372102_comment'></div>县令丞尉杂处民屋。公乃募百姓能以力耕公田者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372102_comment'></div>假之牛梨粟种与食。所收其半与之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372102_comment'></div>不假牛犁者。三分与二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372102_comment'></div>田久不理。草根腐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372102_comment'></div>地增肥。又连遇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1372102", 1372102, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>宜岁</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372102_comment'></div>得粟比馀田亩盈若干。凡积粟三万斛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372102_comment'></div>将复筑室于州故城。令百工之伎以其艺来者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372102_comment'></div>与粟有差。刺史临视给与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372102_comment'></div>吏无所行其私。以故人皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1372102", 1372102, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>便信</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372102_comment'></div>应募者数千人。陶人不知墁而涂有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372102_comment'></div>圬人不板筑而墙有馀。筑人不操斤斧而工有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372102_comment'></div>陶者圬者筑者工者。各以其所能相易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372102_comment'></div>未十旬而城郭室屋建立如初。刺史以官属迁于新城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372102_comment'></div>县令之下。各返其室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372102_comment'></div>创六驿新大市二道四馆器用皆具。曲江县五百人以状诣观察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372102_comment'></div>请作碑立生祠。公自陈所为不足述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372102_comment'></div>假令如百姓言。乃刺史职宜如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372102_comment'></div>何足多者。不愿以小事<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1372102", 1372102, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>市名</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372102_comment'></div>观察使嘉其让。密以状闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372102_comment'></div>迁合州刺史。其始来也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372102_comment'></div>韶之户仅七千。凡六年迁合州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372102_comment'></div>其去也。倍其初之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372102_comment'></div>又盈四千户焉。初先夫人殁于江西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372102_comment'></div>遭贼难未克返葬。寓于西原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372102_comment'></div>公不赴合州。表请奉丧归祔于河南偃师县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372102_comment'></div>既沧景观察使奏请景州刺史阙。其帅辄以其僚属将校自为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372102_comment'></div>不请有年矣。宰相累进刺史名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372102_comment'></div>皆不出。及召公入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372102_comment'></div>言合上旨。遂下诏迁朝散郎使持节景州诸军事景州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372102_comment'></div>充本州团练使兼御史中丞。赐紫金鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372102_comment'></div>寻加节度副使。其明年沧景节度使始朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372102_comment'></div>二年又朝。遂留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372102_comment'></div>诏以其从父兄代之。奏以公充行军司马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372102_comment'></div>公遂以信州府君茔近漕河。表求改葬于重山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372102_comment'></div>诏许之。既徵入京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372102_comment'></div>迁朝散大夫使持节都督邕州诸军事守邕州刺史本管经略招讨使。御史中丞赐紫如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372102_comment'></div>是岁贞元十七年也。诘俚盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372102_comment'></div>除其暴。掠良聚攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372102_comment'></div>禁下如令。通蛮夷道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372102_comment'></div>责土贡。大首领黄氏率其属纳质供赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372102_comment'></div>黄氏周氏韦氏侬氏。皆群盗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372102_comment'></div>黄氏之族最强。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_57_1372102", 1372102, "Clauses/115/Comments/0")'>盘亘</span>十数州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372102_comment'></div>周韦氏之不附之也。率群黄之兵以攻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372102_comment'></div>而逐诸海。黄氏既至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372102_comment'></div>群盗皆服。于是十三部二十九州之蛮宁息无寇害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372102_comment'></div>其明年制迁使持节都督广州诸军事守广州刺史兼御史大夫。充岭南节度观察处置本管经略等使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372102_comment'></div>散官赐如故。前节度使殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372102_comment'></div>掌印吏盗授人职百数。谋夜发兵为乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372102_comment'></div>事觉奔走。公至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372102_comment'></div>阴以术得首恶杀之。不问其馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372102_comment'></div>军中以安。蛮夷俗相攻击群聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372102_comment'></div>缘盗发辄捕斩。无复犯者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372102_comment'></div>蕃国岁来互市。奇珠玳瑁异香文犀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372102_comment'></div>皆浮海舶以来。常贡是供。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372102_comment'></div>不敢有加。舶人安焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372102_comment'></div>商贾以饶。二十一年进阶银青光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372102_comment'></div>元和元年诏加金紫光禄大夫检校礼部尚书。封东海郡开国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1372102_comment'></div>食邑二千户。馀如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1372102_comment'></div>诏书未至。有疾薨于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1372102_comment'></div>凡三佐藩屏之臣。五为刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1372102_comment'></div>一为经略。一为节度观察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1372102_comment'></div>阶累升为金紫光禄大夫。爵超进为开国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1372102_comment'></div>官亟迁为礼部尚书。其事业皆足以传示后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1372102_comment'></div>为子孙法。享年七十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1372102_comment'></div>虽不登于上寿。儒者荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1372102_comment'></div>前夫人渤海高氏。子皆夭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1372102_comment'></div>后夫人扶风窦氏。封国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1372102_comment'></div>有子元弼。前右卫仓曹参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1372102_comment'></div>以读书属文为业。谨具历官行事如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1372102_comment'></div>伏请牒太常编录。谨状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1372102_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_86_1372102_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年11月</a>　寓居洛阳，荐孟郊于河南尹、水陆转运使郑馀庆，孟郊因辟为水陆转运从事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年</a>　寓居洛阳，夏，有文代河南尹郑馀庆作。作品：《祭中天王文》<div id='poem_1372117' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372117' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372117?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭中天王文代河南郑尹作</a><span class='authorDate'>（808年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372117")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372117_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372117'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372117'>自春亢阳。将害嘉谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372117_comment'></div>是以斋心命使。用祈于王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372117_comment'></div>惟神降歆。明应如答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372117_comment'></div>阴云周布。膏泽四施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372117_comment'></div>旱苗复生。宿麦重秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372117_comment'></div>臣人欢悦。草木鲜荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372117_comment'></div>惟王之功。拯祐于下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372117_comment'></div>某忝尹京邑。虑迫群心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372117_comment'></div>实荷王化。道以嘉祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372117_comment'></div>方当月禁。不杀牛羊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372117_comment'></div>谢王嘉锡。曷敢稽留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372117_comment'></div>且荐中素。非陈豆羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372117_comment'></div>请俟踰月。乃列牲牢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372117_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1372117_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=808&endYear=808')">808年10月</a>　寓居洛阳，命受为岭南节度使杨於陵掌书记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年1月18日</a>　去洛阳南行赴任，韩愈、石洪等假舟送行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年1月19日</a>　南行途中，至东洛吊居母丧的孟郊，遂与郊偕行，黄昏至景云山居。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年1月20日</a>　南行途中，晨至佛寺最高处南望嵩山，题姓名纪别，既食，韩孟作别西归。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='39179813cbd848a391bcc803ec19cd04_label'><a href='javascript:
