ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=815&endYear=817')">815-817年</a>，42-44岁</div><div id='39179813cbd848a391bcc803ec19cd04' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=815&endYear=815')">815年</a>　任河南府掾，河北成德节度使王承宗之乱未平，有赋作以舒忧。作品：《幽怀赋并序》<div id='poem_1372016' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372016' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372016?labeling=true' target='_blank'>幽怀赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（815年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372016")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372016_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1372016'>朋友有相叹者。赋幽怀以答之。其辞曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1372016_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372016'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372016'>众<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1372016", 1372016, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>嚣嚣</span>而杂处兮。咸嗟老而羞卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372016_comment'></div>视予心之不然兮。虑行道之犹非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372016_comment'></div>傥中怀之自得兮。终老死其何悲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372016_comment'></div>昔孔门之多贤兮。惟回也为庶几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372016_comment'></div>超群情以独去兮。指圣域而高追。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372016_comment'></div>固箪食与瓢饮兮。宁服轻而驾肥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372016_comment'></div>望若人其如何兮。惭吾德之纤微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372016_comment'></div>躬不田而饱食兮。妻不织而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1372016", 1372016, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>丰衣</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372016_comment'></div>援圣贤而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1372016", 1372016, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>比度</span>兮。何侥倖之能希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372016_comment'></div>念所怀之未展兮。非悼巳而陈私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372016_comment'></div>自禄山之始兵兮。岁周甲而未夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372016_comment'></div>何神尧之郡县兮。乃家传而自持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372016_comment'></div>税生人而育卒兮。列高城以相维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372016_comment'></div>何兹世之可久兮。宜永念而遐思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372016_comment'></div>有三苗之逆命兮。舞干羽以来之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372016_comment'></div>惟刑德之既修兮。无远迩而咸归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372016_comment'></div>当高祖之初起兮。提一旅之羸师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372016_comment'></div>能顺天而用众兮。竟扫寇而戡隋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372016_comment'></div>况天子之神明兮。有烈祖之前规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372016_comment'></div>刬弊政而还本兮。如反掌之易为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372016_comment'></div>苟庙堂之治得兮。何下邑之能违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372016_comment'></div>哀予生之贱远兮。包深怀而告谁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372016_comment'></div>嗟此诚之不达兮。惜此道而无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372016_comment'></div>独中夜以潜叹兮。匪吾忧之所宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372016_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1372016_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　以论事于宰相罢府掾。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=817&endYear=817')">817年</a>　秋，剑南东川节度使卢坦召为从事。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title

-----title
南昌
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='c553bb77c48f48e9aaf198c6e8b322f9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c553bb77c48f48e9aaf198c6e8b322f9");'><span id='c553bb77c48f48e9aaf198c6e8b322f9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年</a>，36岁</div><div id='c553bb77c48f48e9aaf198c6e8b322f9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年4月26日</a>　南行途中，至洪州，遇岭南使游徐孺亭看荷花，有题桄榔亭文。作品：《桄榔亭》<div id='poem_1372085' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372085' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372085?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题桄榔亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（809年4月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372085")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372085_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372085'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372085'>翱与监察御史韦君词皆自东京如岭南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372085_comment'></div>水道仅八千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372085_comment'></div>翱以正月十八日上舟于漕以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372085_comment'></div>韦君期以二月策马疾驱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372085_comment'></div>追我于汴宋之郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372085_comment'></div>或不能及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372085_comment'></div>约自宣城会我于常州以偕行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372085_comment'></div>既翱停舟宿留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372085_comment'></div>日日以须。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372085_comment'></div>韦君之出洛也易期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372085_comment'></div>又宣城谋疾到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372085_comment'></div>逆江南流上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372085_comment'></div>翱以妻疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372085_comment'></div>居信安四十馀日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372085_comment'></div>比及江西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372085_comment'></div>韦君亦前行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372085_comment'></div>上桄榔亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372085_comment'></div>见韦君纪姓名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372085_comment'></div>且有念我之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372085_comment'></div>嗟夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372085_comment'></div>皆行八千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372085_comment'></div>先后之不齐也不过十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372085_comment'></div>而初谋竟乖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372085_comment'></div>人事之不果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372085_comment'></div>不可以前期也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1372085_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
清远
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a992e13dce834764a644f030a9060a7d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a992e13dce834764a644f030a9060a7d");'><span id='a992e13dce834764a644f030a9060a7d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年</a>，36岁</div><div id='a992e13dce834764a644f030a9060a7d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年6月5日</a>　南行途中，在广州境，至清远峡山，游峡山寺，有题峡山文。作品：《题峡山寺》<div id='poem_1372086' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372086' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372086?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题峡山寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（809年6月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372086")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372086_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372086'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372086'>翱为儿童时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372086_comment'></div>闻山游者说峡山寺难为俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372086_comment'></div>远地尝以为无因能来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372086_comment'></div>及兹获游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372086_comment'></div>周历五峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372086_comment'></div>然后知峡山之名有以然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372086_comment'></div>于灵鹫寺时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372086_comment'></div>述诸山居之所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372086_comment'></div>而未言其所不足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372086_comment'></div>如虎邱之剑池不流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372086_comment'></div>天竺之石桥下无泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372086_comment'></div>麓山之力不副天奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372086_comment'></div>灵鹫拥前山不可视远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372086_comment'></div>峡山亦少平地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372086_comment'></div>泉出山无所潭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372086_comment'></div>乃知物之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1372086", 1372086, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>全能</span>难也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372086_comment'></div>况求友择人而欲责全耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372086_comment'></div>去其所阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372086_comment'></div>用其所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372086_comment'></div>则大小之材无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372086_comment'></div>致天下于平治也弗难矣。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1372086_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
广州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e251524183b247ce8712e276b8ac4532_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e251524183b247ce8712e276b8ac4532");'><span id='e251524183b247ce8712e276b8ac4532_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年</a>，36岁</div><div id='e251524183b247ce8712e276b8ac4532' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年6月9日</a>　至广州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年</a>　在广州，有文纪南行经过。作品：《来南录》<div id='poem_1372081' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372081' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372081?labeling=true' target='_blank'>来南录</a><span class='authorDate'>（809年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372081")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372081_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372081'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372081'>元和三年十月。翱既受岭南尚书公之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372081_comment'></div>四年正月己丑。自旌善第以妻子上船于漕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372081_comment'></div>乙未。去东都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372081_comment'></div>韩退之石浚川假舟送子。明日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372081_comment'></div>及故洛东吊孟东野。遂以东野行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372081_comment'></div>浚川以妻疾自漕口先归。黄昏到景云山居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372081_comment'></div>诘朝登上方。南望嵩山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372081_comment'></div>题姓名记别。既食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372081_comment'></div>韩孟别予西归。戊戌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372081_comment'></div>子病寒。饮葱酒以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1372081", 1372081, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>解表</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372081_comment'></div>暮宿于巩。庚子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372081_comment'></div>出洛下河。止汴梁口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372081_comment'></div>遂泛汴流。通河于淮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372081_comment'></div>辛丑。及河阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372081_comment'></div>乙巳。次汴州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372081_comment'></div>疾又加。召医察脉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372081_comment'></div>使人入卢。又二月丁未朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372081_comment'></div>宿陈留。戊申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372081_comment'></div>庄人自卢又来。宿雍邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372081_comment'></div>乙酉。次宋州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372081_comment'></div>疾渐瘳。壬子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372081_comment'></div>至永城。甲寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372081_comment'></div>至埇口。丙辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372081_comment'></div>次泗州。见刺史假舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372081_comment'></div>转淮上河如扬州。庚申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372081_comment'></div>下汴渠入淮。风帆及盱眙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372081_comment'></div>风逆天黑。色波水激。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372081_comment'></div>顺潮入新浦。壬戌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372081_comment'></div>至楚州。丁卯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372081_comment'></div>至扬州。戊辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372081_comment'></div>上栖灵浮图。辛未。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372081_comment'></div>济大江至润州。戊寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372081_comment'></div>至常州。壬午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372081_comment'></div>至苏州。癸未。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372081_comment'></div>如虎邶之山。息足千人石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372081_comment'></div>窥剑池。宿望海楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372081_comment'></div>观走砌石。将游报恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372081_comment'></div>水涸舟不通。无<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1372081", 1372081, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>马道</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372081_comment'></div>不果游。乙酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372081_comment'></div>济松江。丁亥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372081_comment'></div>官艘隙。水溺舟败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372081_comment'></div>戊子。至杭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372081_comment'></div>己丑。如武林之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372081_comment'></div>临曲波观轮桩。登石桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372081_comment'></div>宿高亭。晨望平湖孤山江涛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372081_comment'></div>穷竹道。上新堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372081_comment'></div>周眺群峰。听松风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372081_comment'></div>召灵山永吟叫猿。山童学反舌声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372081_comment'></div>癸巳。驾涛江逆波至富春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372081_comment'></div>丙申。七里滩至睦州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372081_comment'></div>庚子。上杨盈川亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372081_comment'></div>辛丑。至衢州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372081_comment'></div>以妻疾止行。居开元佛寺临江亭后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372081_comment'></div>三月丁未朔。翱在衢州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372081_comment'></div>甲子。女某生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372081_comment'></div>四月丙子朔。翱在衢州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372081_comment'></div>与侯高宿石桥。丙戌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372081_comment'></div>去衢州。戊子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372081_comment'></div>自常山上岭至玉山。庚寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372081_comment'></div>至信州。甲午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372081_comment'></div>望君阳山。怪峰直耸似华山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372081_comment'></div>丙申。上于越亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372081_comment'></div>己亥。直渡担石湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372081_comment'></div>辛丑。至洪州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372081_comment'></div>遇岭南使。游徐孺亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372081_comment'></div>看荷花。五月壬子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372081_comment'></div>至吉州。壬戌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372081_comment'></div>至虔州。己丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372081_comment'></div>与韩泰安平渡江。游灵应山居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372081_comment'></div>辛未。上大庾岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372081_comment'></div>明日。至浈昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372081_comment'></div>癸酉。上灵屯西岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372081_comment'></div>见韶石。甲戌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1372081_comment'></div>宿灵鹫山居。六月乙亥朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1372081_comment'></div>至韶州。丙子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1372081_comment'></div>至始兴公室。戊寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1372081_comment'></div>入东荫山。看大竹笋如婴儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1372081_comment'></div>过浈阳峡。己卯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1372081_comment'></div>宿清远峡山。癸未。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1372081_comment'></div>至广州。自东京至广州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1372081_comment'></div>水道。出衢信七千六百里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1372081_comment'></div>出上元西江七千一百又三十里。自洛州下黄河汴梁过淮至淮阴一千八百有三十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1372081_comment'></div>顺流。自淮阴至邵伯三百有五十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1372081_comment'></div>逆流。自邵伯至江九十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1372081_comment'></div>自润州至杭州八百里。渠有高下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1372081_comment'></div>水皆不流。自杭州至常山六百九十有五里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1372081_comment'></div>逆流。多<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_86_1372081", 1372081, "Clauses/173/Comments/0")'>惊滩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1372081_comment'></div>以竹索引船。乃可上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1372081_comment'></div>自常山至玉山八十里。陆道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1372081_comment'></div>谓之玉山岭。自玉山至湖七百有一十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1372081_comment'></div>顺流。谓之高溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1372081_comment'></div>自湖至洪州一百有一十八里。逆流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1372081_comment'></div>自洪州至大庾岭一千有八百里。逆流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1372081_comment'></div>谓之漳江。自大庾岭至浈昌一百有一十里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1372081_comment'></div>陆道。谓之大庾岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1372081_comment'></div>自浈昌至广州九百有四十里。顺流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1372081_comment'></div>谓之浈江。出韶州谓之韶江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1372081_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1372081_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年</a>　在广州，杨於陵自出钱十万又令幕僚共出钱十万以造石门大雪寺佛殿，李翱连上二状乞请停罢。作品：《与本使杨尚书请停率修寺观钱状、再请停率修寺观钱状》<div id='poem_1372027' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372027' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372027?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与本使杨尚书请停率修寺观钱状</a><span class='authorDate'>（809年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372027")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372027_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372027'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372027'>伏见修寺疏。阁下出钱十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372027_comment'></div>令使院共出十万。以造石门大云寺佛殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372027_comment'></div>翱性本愚。闻道晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372027_comment'></div>窃不谕。阁下以为敛钱造寺必是耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372027_comment'></div>翱虽贫。愿竭家财以助阁下成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372027_comment'></div>如以为未必是耶。阁下官尊望重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372027_comment'></div>凡所举措。宜与后生为法式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372027_comment'></div>安可举一事而不中圣贤之道。以为无害于理耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372027_comment'></div>天下之人。以佛理證心者寡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372027_comment'></div>惟土木铜铁。周于四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372027_comment'></div>残害生人。为逋逃之薮泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372027_comment'></div>阁下以为如有周公仲尼<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1372027", 1372027, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>兴立</span>一王制度。天下寺观僧道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372027_comment'></div>其将兴之乎。其将废之乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372027_comment'></div>若将兴之。是符融梁武皆为仲尼周公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372027_comment'></div>若将废之。阁下又何患其尚寡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372027_comment'></div>而复率其属合力<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1372027", 1372027, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>建置</span>之也。院中判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372027_comment'></div>虽副知巳之命。然利禄远仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372027_comment'></div>亦不以贪也。岂无羁孤亲友由未能力及赒之欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372027_comment'></div>何暇出钱以兴有损无益之务。众情不厌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372027_comment'></div>但奉阁下之命而为耳。拳拳下情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372027_comment'></div>深所未晓。伏惟悯其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1372027", 1372027, "Clauses/41/Comments/0")'>拙浅</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372027_comment'></div>不惜教诲。若阁下所为竟是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372027_comment'></div>翱亦安敢守初心以从而不为也。若其所言有合于道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372027_comment'></div>伏望不重<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1372027", 1372027, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>改成</span>之事。而轻为后生之所议论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372027_comment'></div>意尽辞直。无任战越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372027_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1372027_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
惠州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e69186b679134407b8c75b933ed27255_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e69186b679134407b8c75b933ed27255");'><span id='e69186b679134407b8c75b933ed27255_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=810')">809-810年</a>，36-37岁</div><div id='e69186b679134407b8c75b933ed27255' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=809&endYear=809')">809年11月</a>　以节度使掌书记知循州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年1月</a>　在循州任，迁葬王处士时作文以解人所惑。作品：《解惑》<div id='poem_1372065' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372065' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372065?labeling=true' target='_blank'>解惑</a><span class='authorDate'>（810年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372065")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372065_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372065'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372065'>王野人名体静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372065_comment'></div>盖同州人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372065_comment'></div>始游浮山观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372065_comment'></div>原未有室居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372065_comment'></div>缝纸为裳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372065_comment'></div>取竹架树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372065_comment'></div>覆以草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372065_comment'></div>独止其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372065_comment'></div>豺豹熊象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372065_comment'></div>过而驯之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372065_comment'></div>弗害也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372065_comment'></div>积十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372065_comment'></div>乃构草堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372065_comment'></div>植茶成园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372065_comment'></div>犁田三十亩以供食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372065_comment'></div>不畜妻子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372065_comment'></div>少言说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372065_comment'></div>有所问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372065_comment'></div>尽诚以对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372065_comment'></div>人或取其丝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372065_comment'></div>约酬利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372065_comment'></div>弗问姓名皆与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372065_comment'></div>或负之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372065_comment'></div>终不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372065_comment'></div>凡居二十四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372065_comment'></div>年六十二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372065_comment'></div>贞元二十五年五月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372065_comment'></div>卒于观原茶园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372065_comment'></div>村人相与凿木为空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372065_comment'></div>盛其尸埋于园中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372065_comment'></div>观原积无人居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372065_comment'></div>因野人遂成三百家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372065_comment'></div>有尚怪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372065_comment'></div>因谬谓王野人既死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372065_comment'></div>处士陈恒发其棺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372065_comment'></div>惟见空衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372065_comment'></div>翱与陈相遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372065_comment'></div>问其故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372065_comment'></div>恒曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372065_comment'></div>作记者欲神浮山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372065_comment'></div>故妄云然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372065_comment'></div>元和四年十一月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372065_comment'></div>翱以节度掌书记奉牒知循州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372065_comment'></div>五年正月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372065_comment'></div>准制祭名山大川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372065_comment'></div>翱奉牲牢祭于山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372065_comment'></div>致帝命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372065_comment'></div>遂使斲木为棺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372065_comment'></div>命将吏村人改葬野人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372065_comment'></div>迁于佛寺南冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372065_comment'></div>其骨存焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372065_comment'></div>乃立木于墓东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372065_comment'></div>志曰王处士葬于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372065_comment'></div>削去谬记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372065_comment'></div>以解观听者所惑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1372065_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=810&endYear=810')">810年3月</a>　杨於陵因监军许遂振所谮罢归，李翱亦在此时或稍后北归。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
湖州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='4fa0c68a1b8f44bb927f7a5e5cc1a944_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("4fa0c68a1b8f44bb927f7a5e5cc1a944");'><span id='4fa0c68a1b8f44bb927f7a5e5cc1a944_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=821&endYear=821')">821年12月19日</a>　赴任途中至湖州，第七女足娘卒，十九日有别女足娘墓文。作品：《湖州别女足娘墓文》<div id='poem_1372119' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372119' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372119?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖州别女足娘墓文</a><span class='authorDate'>（821年12月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372119")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372119_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372119'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372119'>维长庆元年岁次辛丑十二月癸亥朔十九日辛巳。父舒州剌史翱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372119_comment'></div>以酒果之奠。敬别于第七女足娘子之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372119_comment'></div>吾以前月二十八日蒙恩改授舒州刺史。以明日将领汝母等水路赴州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372119_comment'></div>故以酒果。来与汝别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372119_comment'></div>呜呼。我为汝父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372119_comment'></div>汝则吾女。王命有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372119_comment'></div>不得安处。延陵丧子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372119_comment'></div>葬不归吴。考之于礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372119_comment'></div>其合矣夫。汝之形骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372119_comment'></div>托终此土。汝之精神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372119_comment'></div>冥漠不睹。上及于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372119_comment'></div>下及于泉。鬼神有知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372119_comment'></div>汝骨安全。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1372119", 1372119, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>永永</span>终古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372119_comment'></div>无有后艰。我来诀别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372119_comment'></div>涕泪涟涟。呜呼尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372119_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1372119_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
潜山
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='59a0b0a6448f482b9d94db0eb112443f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("59a0b0a6448f482b9d94db0eb112443f");'><span id='59a0b0a6448f482b9d94db0eb112443f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=822&endYear=823')">822-823年</a>，49-50岁</div><div id='59a0b0a6448f482b9d94db0eb112443f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=822&endYear=822')">822年</a>　春，莅任舒州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=822&endYear=822')">822年</a>　在舒州任，以绩优赐爵一级，亡母追赠为县夫人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=823&endYear=823')">823年1月</a>　在舒州任，江州刺史李渤筑湖堤竣工，李翱作堤铭。作品：《江州南湖堤铭并序》<div id='poem_1372059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江州南湖堤铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（823年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372059")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1372059_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_1372059'>长庆二年十二月。江州刺史李君浚之截南陂。筑堤三千五百尺。高若干尺。广若干尺。以通四乡之路。畜水为湖。人得其赢。正月既毕事。舒州刺史李翱词以纪之。词曰。</div><div id='poem_preface_1372059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372059'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372059'>天地作物，功或不周。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1372059'>贤人相之，智与神侔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1372059'>漭漭南陂，冬乾夏滮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1372059'>九江暴涨，潜潮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1372059", 1372059, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>逆流</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1372059'>东南百步，城市所繇。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1372059'>水积既深，大波其䬌。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1372059'>亦有舟航，覆溺之忧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1372059'>担壅叠路，车轫其辀。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1372059'>童婴涕堕，老妇号愁。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1372059'>历古迨兹，孰为氓筹。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1372059'>浚之之来，养民如身。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1372059'>乃筑长堤，距江之濒。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1372059'>厚其钱佣，以饱饿人。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1372059'>南北东西，百里斗臻。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1372059'>莫不用力，千锤响振。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1372059'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1372059", 1372059, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>虓欢</span>相励，不督而勤。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1372059'>堤既成止，冈联突起。<div id='poem_sentence_16_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1372059'>坚若石城，障为潴水。<div id='poem_sentence_17_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1372059'>蒲莞菱芡，鸿鸧鳣鲤。<div id='poem_sentence_18_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1372059'>唯其所取，或食或祀。<div id='poem_sentence_19_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1372059'>长堤坦坦，植之杨槐。<div id='poem_sentence_20_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_1372059'>架豁飞圮，以便去来。<div id='poem_sentence_21_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1372059'>除险作利，非贤不能。<div id='poem_sentence_22_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_1372059'>歌示江人，式悦汝怀。<div id='poem_sentence_23_1372059_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1372059'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1372059_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=823&endYear=823')">823年10月</a>　在舒州任。作品：《舒州新堂铭》<div id='poem_1372057' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372057' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372057?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舒州新堂铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（823年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372057")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1372057_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372057'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372057'>先时寝坏，有隘其庐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1372057'>乃作斯堂，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1372057", 1372057, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>高严</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1372057", 1372057, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>旟旟</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1372057'>六桷四楹，装重架虚。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1372057'>栾栱不设，檐蜚祛祛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1372057'>丽不越度，俭而有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1372057'>左立嘉亭，缭以环除。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1372057'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1372057", 1372057, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>延延</span>其深，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1372057", 1372057, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>肆肆</span>其纾。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1372057'>吏事既退，斋心以居。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1372057'>思民之病，择弊而锄。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1372057'>弗逸弗坠，谨终犹初。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1372057'>大旱之后，邻邑成墟。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1372057'>独我州氓，乐哉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1372057", 1372057, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>胥胥</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1372057'>鬼神所福，事匪在予。<div id='poem_sentence_12_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1372057'>丞相所言，乃下徵书。<div id='poem_sentence_13_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1372057'>复官于朝，以解前疽。<div id='poem_sentence_14_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1372057'>刻铭于斯，永示群舒。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1372057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1372057'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1372057_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=823&endYear=823')">823年10月</a>　召为礼部郎中，别舒州前曾著文。作品：《别灊山神文》<div id='poem_1372118' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372118' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372118?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别灊山神文</a><span class='authorDate'>（823年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372118")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372118_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372118'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372118'>维长庆三年十月二十七日。朝议郎守尚书礼部郎中上轻车都尉李翱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372118_comment'></div>谨遣舒州摄要籍司衙前军虞候吴潭。以清酒鹿脯告辞于灊山大神之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372118_comment'></div>翱自去岁。来临此邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372118_comment'></div>遭罹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1372118", 1372118, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>炎旱</span>。淮左毕同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372118_comment'></div>邻郡逃亡。十家六空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372118_comment'></div>惟此舒人。安业于农。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372118_comment'></div>我政无能。遘此岁凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372118_comment'></div>灾同报异。乃神之聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372118_comment'></div>事幸无败。誉斯有融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372118_comment'></div>遂忝帝命。复官南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372118_comment'></div>皆神所祐。我亦何功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372118_comment'></div>将赴京邑。路沿大江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372118_comment'></div>遣使来辞。神鉴予衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372118_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1372118_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
合肥

id='poem_sentence_76_1372106_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=825&endYear=825')">825年</a>　在庐州任，权豪趁干旱、疫病贱买田屋，而穷人仍输租赋，李翱命以田占租，向豪室征税万二千缗。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=825&endYear=825')">825年</a>　在庐州任，有与淮南节度使王播书，言及州郡之乱源于仁义教育之风扫地。作品：《与淮南节度使书》<div id='poem_1372043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与淮南节度使书</a><span class='authorDate'>（825年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372043")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372043_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372043'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372043'>翱自十五已后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372043_comment'></div>即有志于仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372043_comment'></div>见孔子之论高弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372043_comment'></div>未尝不以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1372043", 1372043, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>及物</span>为首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372043_comment'></div>克伐怨欲不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372043_comment'></div>未得为仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372043_comment'></div>管仲不死子纠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372043_comment'></div>复相为雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372043_comment'></div>而功及天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372043_comment'></div>则曰如其仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372043_comment'></div>曰由也果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372043_comment'></div>赐也达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372043_comment'></div>求也艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372043_comment'></div>于从政乎何有。<div id='poem_sentence_15_1372043_comment'></div>教之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372043_comment'></div>父母之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372043_comment'></div>未尝不及于众焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372043_comment'></div>近代已来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372043_comment'></div>俗尚文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372043_comment'></div>由是经之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372043_comment'></div>弃而不求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372043_comment'></div>圣人之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372043_comment'></div>外而不讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372043_comment'></div>干办者为良吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372043_comment'></div>适时者为通贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372043_comment'></div>仁义教育之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372043_comment'></div>于是乎扫地而尽矣。<div id='poem_sentence_34_1372043_comment'></div>州郡之乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372043_comment'></div>又何怪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372043_comment'></div>窃尝病此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372043_comment'></div>以故为官不敢苟求旧例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372043_comment'></div>必探察源本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372043_comment'></div>以恤养为心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372043_comment'></div>以戢豪吏为务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372043_comment'></div>以法令<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1372043", 1372043, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>自检</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372043_comment'></div>以知足自居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372043_comment'></div>利于物者无不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372043_comment'></div>利于私者无不诮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372043_comment'></div>比之时辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372043_comment'></div>亦知颇异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372043_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1372043", 1372043, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>思齐</span>古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372043_comment'></div>则十曾未及其一二为恨耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372043_comment'></div>自到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372043_comment'></div>有改易条上者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372043_comment'></div>亦有细碎侵物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372043_comment'></div>彰从前之失太深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372043_comment'></div>不令条上者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372043_comment'></div>纵未穷尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372043_comment'></div>亦十去其九矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372043_comment'></div>惟三两事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372043_comment'></div>即须使司处置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372043_comment'></div>已有申上者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372043_comment'></div>未蒙裁下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372043_comment'></div>谨具公状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372043_comment'></div>若或并赐处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372043_comment'></div>则当州里无弊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372043_comment'></div>盖古人屈于不知己而伸于知己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372043_comment'></div>翱不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372043_comment'></div>既已谬蒙十一叔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_66_1372043", 1372043, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>知奖</span>如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372043_comment'></div>其又何敢不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372043_comment'></div>翱再拜。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1372043_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
汝南
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fd5e5e58aa8d4ea2b63f822dfe425867_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fd5e5e58aa8d4ea2b63f822dfe425867");'><span id='fd5e5e58aa8d4ea2b63f822dfe425867_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=827&endYear=827')">827年</a>，54岁</div><div id='fd5e5e58aa8d4ea2b63f822dfe425867' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=827&endYear=827')">827年</a>　征为谏议大夫，路出蔡州，因柏元封之托，为其父为作神道碑。作品：《唐故特进左领军卫上将军兼御史大夫平原郡王赠司空柏公神道碑》<div id='poem_1372089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372089?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故特进左领军卫上将军兼御史大夫平原郡王赠司空柏公神道碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（827年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372089")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372089'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372089'>柏氏系自有周。叔虞封晋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372089_comment'></div>其支子有受邑于伯为采地者。因以为姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372089_comment'></div>后世生宗。宗以直显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372089_comment'></div>景公厉公之时。三郤恶宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372089_comment'></div>共谮杀之。其客毕阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372089_comment'></div>以其子州黎奔楚。于是改伯为柏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372089_comment'></div>及汉有鸿者。由议郎为魏郡守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372089_comment'></div>子孙家焉。故为魏郡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372089_comment'></div>有季纂者。入唐为工部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372089_comment'></div>生敬仁为蕲州长史。生謇为河南永宁令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372089_comment'></div>赠大理寺少卿。生造为怀之获嘉令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372089_comment'></div>即公之父也。公讳良器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372089_comment'></div>字公亮。生十二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372089_comment'></div>安禄山陷东郡。获嘉守县印不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372089_comment'></div>为贼将所害。公既免丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372089_comment'></div>怀平贼志。乃学击剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372089_comment'></div>依父友王奂。奂尝曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372089_comment'></div>汝额文似李临淮。面黑子似颜平原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372089_comment'></div>其必立。临淮即太尉光弼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372089_comment'></div>年十七。得汝州龙兴尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372089_comment'></div>王奂从事太尉府。荐之太尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372089_comment'></div>召与言。遂授以兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372089_comment'></div>使平安越之盗。累授左武卫中郎将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372089_comment'></div>以所将兵隶于浙西。广德岁中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372089_comment'></div>盗陷江东十州。公帅所将兵来婺州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372089_comment'></div>功多进左武卫将军。平方清于洞中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372089_comment'></div>赐钱五百万。破张三霸海上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372089_comment'></div>改左金吾卫将军。为都知兵马使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372089_comment'></div>大历初。潘狞虎据小伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372089_comment'></div>胡参据蒸里。江东大扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372089_comment'></div>公将卒三千人骑五百人与战。皆破之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372089_comment'></div>斩首三千级。执俘一千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372089_comment'></div>诏加检校光禄大夫兼苏州别驾。又加左羽林大将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372089_comment'></div>试殿中监察御史李栖筠问公年。对曰二十有四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372089_comment'></div>战阵几何。曰六十有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372089_comment'></div>李公叹曰。相识甚近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372089_comment'></div>得公甚深。勉哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372089_comment'></div>公泣涕谢曰。遭时丧乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372089_comment'></div>父死家破。誓弃性命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372089_comment'></div>以除寇雠。私志未立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372089_comment'></div>岂敢望为明公之所知哉。建中初尝至京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372089_comment'></div>宰相杨炎召之语。公因言两河有事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372089_comment'></div>职税所办者。惟在江东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372089_comment'></div>李道昌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1372089", 1372089, "Clauses/86/Comments/0")'>无政</span>。宜速得人以代之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372089_comment'></div>炎许诺。其冬遂并宣越与浙西以为一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372089_comment'></div>而以晋州剌史韩滉代道昌焉。及德宗如梁州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372089_comment'></div>李希烈陷汴州。逐李勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372089_comment'></div>遂僭帝号。寇陈州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372089_comment'></div>围宋宁陵。滉使公将卒万人救陈并宁陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372089_comment'></div>是时刘元佐败于白塔。收其卒保宋州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372089_comment'></div>使将王彦昭守宁陵。希烈拥水灌其南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372089_comment'></div>筑埇道亲临其北。令军中曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372089_comment'></div>明日日中陷城。公闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372089_comment'></div>厉所将兵。成阵以进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372089_comment'></div>恐城陷不及。使弩手善游者五百人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372089_comment'></div>沿汴渠夜进。去城数里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372089_comment'></div>没于水中。遂得入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372089_comment'></div>及旦。贼驱勇卒登城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372089_comment'></div>城中伏弩悉发。皆贯人毙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372089_comment'></div>其后希烈始知救兵得入。杀守将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372089_comment'></div>因罢去。将昌集城中人哭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372089_comment'></div>向非浙西救至。则此城已屠矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372089_comment'></div>遂拔襄邑。收漳口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372089_comment'></div>宋州由是获全。李希烈遂失汴州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372089_comment'></div>奔于蔡。诏封平原郡王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372089_comment'></div>食邑三千户。特进兼御史中丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372089_comment'></div>贞元二年淮西平。诏曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372089_comment'></div>休勋茂伐。书于竹帛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372089_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_68_1372089", 1372089, "Clauses/136/Comments/0")'>戎籍</span>乃为裨将副。非所以褒功宠德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372089_comment'></div>其以为左神策军将军知军事兼官如故。五年诏与太尉晟侍中瑊等三十六人图形于凌烟阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372089_comment'></div>上亲御。即其形而赞之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372089_comment'></div>八年迁大将军。士卒之在市贩者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372089_comment'></div>悉挥斥去。募勇者代之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1372089_comment'></div>故为所监者不悦。明年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1372089_comment'></div>公之故人有犯禁宿于望仙门者。卫使奏言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1372089_comment'></div>遂转右领军卫大将军。所监者乃用其衙将魏循代为将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1372089_comment'></div>自是军中之政。不复在于将军矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1372089_comment'></div>十五年兼英武将军使。十八年迁左领军兼御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1372089_comment'></div>十九年闰十月。以疾卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1372089_comment'></div>年六十一。天子为之废朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1372089_comment'></div>赠陕州大都督。明年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1372089_comment'></div>葬于万年毕原。夫人康氏先殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1372089_comment'></div>后始附葬。有子曰元封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1372089_comment'></div>为蔡州剌史。曰耆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1372089_comment'></div>为谏议大夫。曰元凤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1372089_comment'></div>为澄城主簿。曰夔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1372089_comment'></div>为襄州参军。三女皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1372089_comment'></div>以元封及耆累赠为司空。夫人追封魏国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1372089_comment'></div>初公与王栖曜李长荣皆事韩晋公。栖曜至鄜坊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1372089_comment'></div>长荣至河阳泽潞。皆拥节有土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1372089_comment'></div>公自少则戮力破贼。及壮解宁陵猗杖之围。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1372089_comment'></div>希烈之所以兵不及于宋。而江东以全者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1372089_comment'></div>实公之所为也。功最高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1372089_comment'></div>位独以不副。克生良子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1372089_comment'></div>能大厥家。太和元年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1372089_comment'></div>翱自庐以谏议大夫徵。路出于蔡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1372089_comment'></div>元封泣拜。且曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1372089_comment'></div>先公之碑未树。教后嗣其果有辞俟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1372089_comment'></div>公不可听。乃铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1372089_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_99_1372089'>公生十二。未壮家毁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1372089_comment'></div>誓殄父雠。不怯勇死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1372089_comment'></div>释官就军。焯有其勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1372089_comment'></div>擒凶盗平。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_102_1372089", 1372089, "Clauses/205/Comments/0")'>威明</span>显闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1372089_comment'></div>人谁不贵。孰胜其位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1372089_comment'></div>由卑至巨。莫匪躬致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1372089_comment'></div>宣疏土疆。报未功当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1372089_comment'></div>是生后人。绍庆不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1372089_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_107_1372089_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
郑州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9779d42ca4b7457da544a01a9d4b6f6a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9779d42ca4b7457da544a01a9d4b6f6a");'><span id='9779d42ca4b7457da544a01a9d4b6f6a_link'
