ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年</a>　在郑州任，是年前后有诗赠郑州管城县令。作品：《戏赠诗》<div id='poem_30349' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_30349' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/30349?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戏赠诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（831年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_30349")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_30349_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_30349'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_30349'>县君好砖渠，绕水恣行游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_30349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_30349'>鄙性乐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_30349", 30349, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>疏野</span>，凿地便成沟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_30349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_30349'>两岸值芳草，中央漾清流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_30349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_30349'>所尚既不同，砖凿可自修。<div id='poem_sentence_3_30349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_30349'>从他后人见，境趣谁为幽。<div id='poem_sentence_4_30349_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_30349'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_30349_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年4月</a>　在郑州任，四月葬杨於陵于郑州，李翱有祭文并作墓志。作品：《祭杨仆射文》《唐故金紫光禄大夫尚书右仆射致仕上柱国宏农郡开国公食邑二千户赠司空杨公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1372110' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372110' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372110?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭杨仆射文</a><span class='authorDate'>（831年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372110")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372110_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372110'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372110'>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372110_comment'></div>贞元中岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372110_comment'></div>公既为郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372110_comment'></div>始获趋门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372110_comment'></div>仰公之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372110_comment'></div>遂假荐言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372110_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1372110", 1372110, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>幽蛰</span>用彰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372110_comment'></div>德惠之厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372110_comment'></div>殁身敢忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372110_comment'></div>公以直道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372110_comment'></div>于南出藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372110_comment'></div>谬管记室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372110_comment'></div>日陪讨论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372110_comment'></div>旧政多秕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372110_comment'></div>如丝之棼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372110_comment'></div>与贤共谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372110_comment'></div>秽涤榛燔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372110_comment'></div>监戎戾强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372110_comment'></div>阴附包奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372110_comment'></div>潜谮危疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372110_comment'></div>处之若闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372110_comment'></div>并兼百流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372110_comment'></div>清浊中分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372110_comment'></div>宾主之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372110_comment'></div>由兹益敦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372110_comment'></div>公自登朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372110_comment'></div>及于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1372110", 1372110, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>谢政</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372110_comment'></div>善接交友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372110_comment'></div>居官<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_28_1372110", 1372110, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>恪敬</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372110_comment'></div>温然如春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372110_comment'></div>柔立不佞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372110_comment'></div>坐直屡退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372110_comment'></div>进匪由竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372110_comment'></div>更历中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372110_comment'></div>声华日盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372110_comment'></div>咸期作相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372110_comment'></div>为国之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372110_comment'></div>宜而不居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372110_comment'></div>斯可云命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372110_comment'></div>知足<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_39_1372110", 1372110, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>告休</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372110_comment'></div>颐养于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372110_comment'></div>子为侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372110_comment'></div>光耀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1372110", 1372110, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>芬葩</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372110_comment'></div>亦列卿曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372110_comment'></div>秩禄且多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372110_comment'></div>孙童满前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372110_comment'></div>园沼经过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372110_comment'></div>门吏盈朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372110_comment'></div>宴赏有加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372110_comment'></div>宜哉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1372110", 1372110, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>万寿</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372110_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1372110", 1372110, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>吉庆</span>靡他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372110_comment'></div>弃此弗顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372110_comment'></div>哀哉奈何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372110_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372110_comment'></div>身谁不贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372110_comment'></div>有后斯荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372110_comment'></div>惟公之嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372110_comment'></div>实大家声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372110_comment'></div>公为弗亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372110_comment'></div>显显其名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372110_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372110_comment'></div>卜筮叶期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372110_comment'></div>返宅于荥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372110_comment'></div>翱复守郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372110_comment'></div>居不敢宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372110_comment'></div>追怀恩旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372110_comment'></div>躬在郊坰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372110_comment'></div>承教绝绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372110_comment'></div>刻扬德馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372110_comment'></div>缟服前导。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372110_comment'></div>尽哀<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1372110", 1372110, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>墓庭</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372110_comment'></div>尚或鉴此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372110_comment'></div>公乎有灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1372110_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1372110_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_74_1372110_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1372092' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372092' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372092?labeling=true' target='_blank'>唐故金紫光禄大夫尚书右仆射致仕上柱国宏农郡开国公食邑二千户赠司空杨公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（831年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372092")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372092_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372092'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372092'>由杨喜追杀项羽。以功封侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372092_comment'></div>后数世生敞。官至丞相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372092_comment'></div>敞曾孙宝。不应王莽之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372092_comment'></div>光武特徵。老病不到。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372092_comment'></div>宝生震。诸儒谓之关西孔子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372092_comment'></div>位至大司徒太尉。卒以忠死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372092_comment'></div>杨氏由是益大。载于史传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372092_comment'></div>世不绝人。曾祖圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372092_comment'></div>辰州司户。赠膳部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372092_comment'></div>大父冠俗。奉先县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372092_comment'></div>赠吏部郎中。父太清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372092_comment'></div>宋州单父县尉。累赠至太保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372092_comment'></div>公讳于陵。字达夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372092_comment'></div>年十八举进士第。选补润州句容主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372092_comment'></div>鄂岳观察使奏为判官。转左骁卫兵曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372092_comment'></div>累改评事监察御史。历殿中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372092_comment'></div>得绯衣银鱼。使迁江西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372092_comment'></div>公随之。加侍御史著作郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372092_comment'></div>及府除。屏居建昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372092_comment'></div>不至京师。贞元八年徵拜膳部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372092_comment'></div>转考功。知别头举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372092_comment'></div>转吏部员外郎。及判南曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372092_comment'></div>宰相之亲。有以文书不足駮去者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372092_comment'></div>宰相召吏人诘之。坚执不改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372092_comment'></div>遂以公为宣武吊祭使。故事南曹郎未尝有出使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372092_comment'></div>公既出。宰相之亲由是判成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372092_comment'></div>故公卒不得在诏诰之清选。遂为右司郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372092_comment'></div>郎官惰于宿直。临直多以假免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372092_comment'></div>公白右丞。建立条例。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372092_comment'></div>郎官不悦。为作口语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372092_comment'></div>宰相有知其事者。遽以公为吏部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372092_comment'></div>改京兆少尹。出为绛州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372092_comment'></div>有言公弗当居外者。德宗召见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372092_comment'></div>遂以为中书舍人。其年知吏部选事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372092_comment'></div>时京兆尹李实有宠。去不附己者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372092_comment'></div>故给事中许孟容为太常少卿。而公改秘书少监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372092_comment'></div>德宗崩。为太原幽镇等十道告哀使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372092_comment'></div>持节之遗。并辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372092_comment'></div>复命。除华州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372092_comment'></div>赐三品衣鱼。所取宾僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372092_comment'></div>皆一时名人。后皆显官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372092_comment'></div>有至宰相者。其年冬迁浙江东道团练观察使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372092_comment'></div>越中大饥。人至相食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372092_comment'></div>公奏请度支米三十万斛。又乞籴他道以赈救之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372092_comment'></div>民得生全。入为户部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372092_comment'></div>未到改京兆尹。奏请诸军使有犯罪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372092_comment'></div>皆禁身推罪。以状牒送本军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372092_comment'></div>又请属诸军诸使人置挟名敕五丁者。推两丁属军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372092_comment'></div>递立节限。以便于治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372092_comment'></div>诏皆可其奏。京师称之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372092_comment'></div>复为户部侍郎。人望益重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372092_comment'></div>佥以公遂为宰相。会考制举人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372092_comment'></div>奖直言策为第一。中贵人大怒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372092_comment'></div>宰相有欲因而出之者。由是为岭南节度使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372092_comment'></div>是时得考策者凡四人。公既得岭南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1372092_comment'></div>员外郎韦贯之再贬巴州刺史。而李益郑敬皆抵于患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1372092_comment'></div>其在广州。以韦词为节度判官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1372092_comment'></div>任之以政。改易侵人之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1372092_comment'></div>凡一十有七。岭外之人至兹传道之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1372092_comment'></div>节度使徐申以己俸薄。月加三十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1372092_comment'></div>且曰。后来所期共守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1372092_comment'></div>公引常衮所奏敕皆罢之。撤去蒲葵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1372092_comment'></div>陶瓦覆屋。遂无火灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1372092_comment'></div>民赖以安。监军许遂振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1372092_comment'></div>好货戾彊。而小人有阴附之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1372092_comment'></div>故遂振密表谮公。直言韦词李翱惑乱军政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1372092_comment'></div>于是除替罢归。遂振既领后事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1372092_comment'></div>捶挞吏人。求公之非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1372092_comment'></div>吏人大声呼曰。杨尚书他方所遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1372092_comment'></div>尚不收去。岂有侵用官钱乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1372092_comment'></div>遂振遽令取他方所遗。及其既至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1372092_comment'></div>封印不启。遂振惭而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1372092_comment'></div>宰相裴垍素未知公。及遂振之谮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1372092_comment'></div>遂以公为吏部侍郎。重修<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_73_1372092", 1372092, "Clauses/147/Comments/0")'>甲敕</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1372092_comment'></div>用备奸源。又于南曹更置别历。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1372092_comment'></div>以相检覆。奏令选人纳直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1372092_comment'></div>为出<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_76_1372092", 1372092, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>签告</span>以给之。吏息奸欺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1372092_comment'></div>官收羡钱。公食丰絜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1372092_comment'></div>廨宇以修。迄兹守行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1372092_comment'></div>遂为故事。凡历四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1372092_comment'></div>补内外官三千馀员。皆当其分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1372092_comment'></div>无怨诉者。转兵部侍郎兼御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1372092_comment'></div>判度支。当淮西用兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1372092_comment'></div>漕挽供馈。盐铁积欠官钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1372092_comment'></div>与之廷辩。高霞寓以唐邓之师攻蔡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1372092_comment'></div>怯懦不敢直进。欲南抵申州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1372092_comment'></div>出于空虚不守之地。其路险狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1372092_comment'></div>粮运难继。公面于上前累言利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1372092_comment'></div>并以疏陈霞寓逗遛之状。请于北道直进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1372092_comment'></div>足以援许汝之师。贼势自蹙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1372092_comment'></div>上许之。霞寓深怨之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1372092_comment'></div>遂内外<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_91_1372092", 1372092, "Clauses/182/Comments/0")'>结构</span>。出为郴州刺史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1372092_comment'></div>霞寓果败。由是谈者知公之冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1372092_comment'></div>其为郴州。躬勤于治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1372092_comment'></div>不以卑远为薄。明年召拜原王傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1372092_comment'></div>数日又为户部侍郎。复知吏部选事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1372092_comment'></div>元和十四年淄青平。兼御史大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1372092_comment'></div>以本官充东平宣慰处置使。是时初诛李师道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1372092_comment'></div>得兖郓州等十二州。列为三道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1372092_comment'></div>刘悟既除滑州。犹未出郓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1372092_comment'></div>及公至。悟出迎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1372092_comment'></div>公促之。悟即日遂发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1372092_comment'></div>颁行赏赐。皆得其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1372092_comment'></div>上甚悦。谓宰臣曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1372092_comment'></div>杨某不易得。及浙西观察使李脩死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1372092_comment'></div>上问宰臣崔群皇甫镈曰。何不进浙西人名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1372092_comment'></div>皇甫镈知公方有恩。惧作相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1372092_comment'></div>遂言公所至皆有理绩。以臣所见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1372092_comment'></div>莫如杨某。凡数百言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1372092_comment'></div>上惟以一字应之曰惜。人闻之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1372092_comment'></div>且以必为相矣。是时裴门下既出太原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1372092_comment'></div>崔中书为镈所谮。镈又改尊号中上旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1372092_comment'></div>故镈计竟行。而公不相矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1372092_comment'></div>明年迁户部尚书。又一年改太常卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1372092_comment'></div>又一年改东都留守兼兵部尚书御史大夫。充蕲汝都防御使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1372092_comment'></div>既三年。方将告休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1372092_comment'></div>会以疾而罢。乃叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1372092_comment'></div>年老致政。本吾夙志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1372092_comment'></div>兹则负吾平生心矣。疾平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1372092_comment'></div>迁检校左仆射兼太子少傅。或劝求分司以自便者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1372092_comment'></div>公曰。年至力惫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1372092_comment'></div>便当乞骸骨于朝。何用分司为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1372092_comment'></div>遂西至京师。朝谢讫不到中书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1372092_comment'></div>遂还私家。不判上案。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1372092_comment'></div>三上表乞自退。诏迁左仆射致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1372092_comment'></div>全给俸料。数月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1372092_comment'></div>上表固让。乞就半俸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1372092_comment'></div>许之。庙享之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1372092_comment'></div>不复经过人家。每佳辰体安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1372092_comment'></div>则以子弟孙僮侍游于园沼之中。用以为适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1372092_comment'></div>太和四年十二月癸亥。以疾薨于新昌第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1372092_comment'></div>享年七十有八。天子为之废朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1372092_comment'></div>凡朝廷之贤。设位而哭者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1372092_comment'></div>不知几人。册赠司空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1372092_comment'></div>明年四月庚午。归葬郑州荥泽县先太保之兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1372092_comment'></div>祔于颍川韩氏赠华阴郡太夫人之茔。夫人丞相少师休之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1372092_comment'></div>丞相晋国公滉之女。柔顺之德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1372092_comment'></div>纪于前铭。下从舅姑四十有三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1372092_comment'></div>子景复。卫尉卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1372092_comment'></div>曰嗣复。户部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1372092_comment'></div>曰绍复。举进士登宏词科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1372092_comment'></div>曰师复。未仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1372092_comment'></div>用文为业。女适右司郎中韦公素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1372092_comment'></div>孙承涣。试大理评事鄜坊节度巡官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1372092_comment'></div>承涣之下及在童稚者十有一人。大卿侍郎以翱之受恩也久。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1372092_comment'></div>来请为志。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1372092_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_146_1372092'>公生六年。太保<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_146_1372092", 1372092, "Clauses/293/Comments/0")'>弃捐</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1372092_comment'></div>未及成童。虢国又终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1372092_comment'></div>漂泊江湖。谁食谁衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1372092_comment'></div>服习文学。不劳于师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1372092_comment'></div>爰始有名。既于永归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1372092_comment'></div>六十一年。祗慎德仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1372092_comment'></div>由直屡黜。进无异词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1372092_comment'></div>凡所临莅。去而可思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1372092_comment'></div>与之厚者。莫匪隽材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1372092_comment'></div>自我进者。多遇良能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1372092_comment'></div>恩建葭莩。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_156_1372092", 1372092, "Clauses/313/Comments/0")'>濡洽</span>以财。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1372092_comment'></div>袒免缌麻。亦尽其哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1372092_comment'></div>止足告归。偃息丘园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1372092_comment'></div>子裔孙童。十有五人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1372092_comment'></div>有列卿曹。贵为侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1372092_comment'></div>禄秩且多。膳饮馨香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1372092_comment'></div>门吏诸生。中外显光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1372092_comment'></div>车马盈门。岁时之良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1372092_comment'></div>既寿且贵。示终以常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1372092_comment'></div>福荐攸归。畴可比望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1372092_comment'></div>为庙太祖。百世蒸尝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1372092_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_167_1372092_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年</a>　在郑州任，夏，李渤卒，有祭文。作品：《祭李宾客文》<div id='poem_1372111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372111?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭李宾客文</a><span class='authorDate'>（831年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372111")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372111_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372111'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372111'>呜呼。天地粹气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372111_comment'></div>降为哲人。忠播大惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372111_comment'></div>济于生民。命与时违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372111_comment'></div>有此不伸。责安所归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372111_comment'></div>乃在鬼神。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372111_comment'></div>兄初有疾。隶人来告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372111_comment'></div>走驷往视。连呼不觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372111_comment'></div>痛搅我肠。谁其能疗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372111_comment'></div>嫂侄既至。患亦微痊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372111_comment'></div>我时屡往。笑语依然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372111_comment'></div>实希返初。以及高年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372111_comment'></div>谪官分曹。拜恩遄发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372111_comment'></div>负罪即路。不遑去别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372111_comment'></div>意谓全德。功当及人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372111_comment'></div>尚祈会面。复接欢忻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372111_comment'></div>如何一乖。死生骤分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372111_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。岂虞浚之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372111_comment'></div>遂臻于兹。舍我而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372111_comment'></div>将安取规。惟后与先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372111_comment'></div>能校几时。短耶长耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372111_comment'></div>终永同归。死为尽乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372111_comment'></div>将有所之。惟尽惟有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372111_comment'></div>兄其己知。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372111_comment'></div>兄之既疾。告于妻子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372111_comment'></div>自古神圣。莫不皆尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372111_comment'></div>名垂不灭。能光万祀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372111_comment'></div>生平交故。殁后谁是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372111_comment'></div>吾友在东。可以托死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372111_comment'></div>且吾所有。往谓编纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372111_comment'></div>吾名庶存。乃贤在史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372111_comment'></div>临绝又告。丁宁心耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372111_comment'></div>所录既到。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1372111", 1372111, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>酸惨</span>启书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372111_comment'></div>披寻未穷。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1372111", 1372111, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>漫洟</span>盈裾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372111_comment'></div>生虽相好。殁更有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372111_comment'></div>敢辞厚命。但恶空虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372111_comment'></div>著兄之德。刻石幽墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372111_comment'></div>传乎万祀。用显名誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372111_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。兄丧东来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372111_comment'></div>我拘郡事。□□□□棺不得视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372111_comment'></div>形存心游。荡魄伤气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372111_comment'></div>一杯写情。四望歔欷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372111_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。尚飨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372111_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1372111_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年12月</a>　除桂州刺史充桂管观察使。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
长沙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='5c367b18083149cab149db5c9e453ddb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5c367b18083149cab149db5c9e453ddb");'><span id='5c367b18083149cab149db5c9e453ddb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=834')">833-834年</a>，60-61岁</div><div id='5c367b18083149cab149db5c9e453ddb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　在潭州任，与书中书舍人李珏，有意休官。作品：《与翰林李舍人书》<div id='poem_1372047' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1372047' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1372047?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与翰林李舍人书</a><span class='authorDate'>（833年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 中唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(17014, "中唐", "李翱", "poem_title_1372047")'>李翱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1372047_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1372047'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1372047'>翱思逃后祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1372047_comment'></div>所冀存身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1372047_comment'></div>惟能<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1372047", 1372047, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>休罢</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1372047_comment'></div>最惬私志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1372047_comment'></div>从此永已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1372047_comment'></div>更无健羡之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1372047_comment'></div>况乞得馀年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1372047_comment'></div>退修至道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1372047_comment'></div>上可以追赤松子房之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1372047_comment'></div>岂止于比二疏尚平子而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1372047_comment'></div>但举世好爵禄权柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1372047_comment'></div>具写此心以告人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1372047_comment'></div>人无有少信之者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1372047_comment'></div>皆为不诚之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1372047_comment'></div>王拾遗是桂州旧僚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1372047_comment'></div>颇知此志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1372047_comment'></div>若与往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1372047_comment'></div>伏望问之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1372047_comment'></div>可知其旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1372047_comment'></div>但以常情见待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1372047_comment'></div>岂知失时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1372047_comment'></div>还有偏尚之士哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1372047_comment'></div>又近日来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1372047_comment'></div>两施子粗得其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1372047_comment'></div>未及就正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1372047_comment'></div>当此时使获长往。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1372047_comment'></div>亦足以不愧宗门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1372047_comment'></div>不负朋友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1372047_comment'></div>尝慕张公以不能取容当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1372047_comment'></div>故终身不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1372047_comment'></div>况向前仕宦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1372047_comment'></div>亦以多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1372047_comment'></div>幸免刑戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1372047_comment'></div>方尔退修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1372047_comment'></div>与致令名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1372047_comment'></div>年已六十有一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1372047_comment'></div>比之诸叔父兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1372047_comment'></div>为得年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1372047_comment'></div>且不知馀年几何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1372047_comment'></div>意愿乞取残年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1372047_comment'></div>以修所知之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1372047_comment'></div>如或有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1372047_comment'></div>是万世一遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1372047_comment'></div>纵使无成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1372047_comment'></div>且能早知止足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1372047_comment'></div>高静与三老死于林薮之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1372047_comment'></div>比终日矻矻耽乐富贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1372047_comment'></div>而大功德不及于海内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1372047_comment'></div>而卒于位者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1372047_comment'></div>所失得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1372047_comment'></div>伏计舍人必以辨之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1372047_comment'></div>以舍人比他见知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1372047_comment'></div>故尽其意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1372047_comment'></div>若非至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1372047_comment'></div>亦何苦而强发斯言乎。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1372047_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=834&endYear=834')">834年</a>　在潭州任，是年或稍前尝遇故苏州刺史韦夏卿之女沦为舞妓，李翱为其选士而嫁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=834&endYear=834')">834年12月</a>　选为刑部侍郎。<br /></div>
-----end

襄阳
